\doxysubsection{Description détaillée}
PHP class for generating PDF documents without requiring external extensions. \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f}{TCPDF} project (\href{http://www.tcpdf.org}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+tcpdf.\+org}}) has been originally derived in 2002 from the Public \doxylink{class_domain}{Domain} FPDF class by Olivier Plathey (\href{http://www.fpdf.org}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+fpdf.\+org}}), but now is almost entirely rewritten.~\newline
 

\doxysubsection{Documentation des constructeurs et destructeur}
\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_ad9c7865a75fb9ee51d4b8188afd00192}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_ad9c7865a75fb9ee51d4b8188afd00192} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!\_\_construct@{\_\_construct}}
\index{\_\_construct@{\_\_construct}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_\_construct()}{\_\_construct()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+construct (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$orientation = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{P}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$unit = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{mm}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$format = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{A4}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$unicode = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$encoding = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{UTF}}-\/8\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$diskcache = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$pdfa = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This is the class constructor. It allows to set up the page format, the orientation and the measure unit used in all the methods (except for the font sizes).


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$orientation} & page orientation. Possible values are (case insensitive)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item P or Portrait (default)
\item L or Landscape
\item \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} (empty string) for automatic orientation
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$unit} & \doxylink{class_user}{User} measure unit. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item pt\+: point
\item mm\+: millimeter (default)
\item cm\+: centimeter
\item in\+: inch
\end{DoxyItemize}~\newline
A point equals 1/72 of inch, that is to say about 0.\+35 mm (an inch being 2.\+54 cm). This is a very common unit in typography; font sizes are expressed in that unit. \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$format} & The format used for pages. It can be either\+: one of the string values specified at get\+Page\+Size\+From\+Format() or an array of parameters specified at \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a31727d77336d2e92a731d4322ed62f46}{set\+Page\+Format()}. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$unicode} & TRUE means that the input text is unicode (default = true) \\
\hline
string & {\em \$encoding} & Charset encoding (used only when converting back html entities); default is UTF-\/8. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$diskcache} & DEPRECATED FEATURE \\
\hline
false | integer & {\em \$pdfa} & If not false, set the document to PDF/A mode and the good version (1 or 3).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
get\+Page\+Size\+From\+Format(), \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a31727d77336d2e92a731d4322ed62f46}{set\+Page\+Format()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

Append a cubic Bezier curve to the current path. The curve shall extend from the current point to the point (x3, y3), using (x1, y1) and (x2, y2) as the Bezier control points. The new current point shall be (x3, y3).

\hline

\hline

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_outellipticalarc()}{\_outellipticalarc()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \+\_\+outellipticalarc (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$xc,  }\item[{}]{\$yc,  }\item[{}]{\$rx,  }\item[{}]{\$ry,  }\item[{}]{\$xang = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$angs = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$angf = {\ttfamily 360},  }\item[{}]{\$pie = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$nc = {\ttfamily 2},  }\item[{}]{\$startpoint = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$ccw = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$svg = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Append an elliptical arc to the current path. An ellipse is formed from n Bezier curves. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$xc} & Abscissa of center point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$yc} & Ordinate of center point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$rx} & Horizontal radius. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$ry} & Vertical radius (if ry = 0 then is a circle, see \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a29f78edbfd2dfd19e9d6d0b6d329807c}{Circle()}). Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$xang} & Angle between the X-\/axis and the major axis of the ellipse. Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$angs} & Angle start of draw line. Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$angf} & Angle finish of draw line. Default value\+: 360. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$pie} & if true do not mark the border point (used to draw pie sectors). \\
\hline
integer & {\em \$nc} & Number of curves used to draw a 90 degrees portion of ellipse. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$startpoint} & if true output a starting point. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ccw} & if true draws in counter-\/clockwise. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$svg} & if true the angles are in svg mode (already calculated). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
array bounding box coordinates (x min, y min, x max, y max) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
4.\+9.\+019 (2010-\/04-\/26)

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!AcceptPageBreak@{AcceptPageBreak}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AcceptPageBreak()}{AcceptPageBreak()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Accept\+Page\+Break (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Whenever a page break condition is met, the method is called, and the break is issued or not depending on the returned value. The default implementation returns a value according to the mode selected by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Auto\+Page\+Break()}.~\newline
 This method is called automatically and should not be called directly by the application. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
bool
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+4 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a1a0390351695ec7f1a9c01d88d303a87}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a1a0390351695ec7f1a9c01d88d303a87} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!AddFont@{AddFont}}
\index{AddFont@{AddFont}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AddFont()}{AddFont()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Add\+Font (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$family,  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fontfile = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$subset = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{default}}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Imports a True\+Type, Type1, core, or CID0 font and makes it available. It is necessary to generate a font definition file first (read /fonts/utils/\+README.TXT). The definition file (and the font file itself when embedding) must be present either in the current directory or in the one indicated by K\+\_\+\+PATH\+\_\+\+FONTS if the constant is defined. If it could not be found, the error "{}\+Could not include font definition file"{} is generated. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$family} & Font family. The name can be chosen arbitrarily. If it is a standard family name, it will override the corresponding font. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Font style. Possible values are (case insensitive)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item empty string\+: regular (default)
\item B\+: bold
\item I\+: italic
\item BI or IB\+: bold italic
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$fontfile} & The font definition file. By default, the name is built from the family and style, in lower case with no spaces. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
array\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}false array containing the font data, or false in case of error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
mixed & {\em \$subset} & if true embedd only a subset of the font (stores only the information related to the used characters); if false embedd full font; if \textquotesingle{}default\textquotesingle{} uses the default value set using \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a8b5e171af1fa013b2cda7ec6005af7c0}{set\+Font\+Subsetting()}. This option is valid only for True\+Type\+Unicode fonts. If you want to enable users to change the document, set this parameter to false. If you subset the font, the person who receives your PDF would need to have your same font in order to make changes to your PDF. The file size of the PDF would also be smaller because you are embedding only part of a font.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+5 
\end{DoxySince}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Font()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a8b5e171af1fa013b2cda7ec6005af7c0}{set\+Font\+Subsetting()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!addHtmlLink@{addHtmlLink}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addHtmlLink()}{addHtmlLink()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily add\+Html\+Link (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$url,  }\item[{}]{\$name,  }\item[{}]{\$fill = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$firstline = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$color = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{}]{\$firstblock = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Output anchor link. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$url} & link URL or internal link (i.\+e.\+: \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}a href="{}\#23,4.\+5"{}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}link to page 23 at 4.\+5 Y position\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}/a\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}) \\
\hline
string & {\em \$name} & link name \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fill} & Indicates if the cell background must be painted (true) or transparent (false). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$firstline} & if true prints only the first line and return the remaining string. \\
\hline
array | null & {\em \$color} & array of RGB text color \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & font style (U, D, B, I) \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$firstblock} & if true the string is the starting of a line. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
int the number of cells used or the remaining text if \$firstline = true; 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a589373b0e23d2effd6a03af3b9b91a35}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a589373b0e23d2effd6a03af3b9b91a35} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!addHTMLTOC@{addHTMLTOC}}
\index{addHTMLTOC@{addHTMLTOC}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addHTMLTOC()}{addHTMLTOC()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily add\+HTMLTOC (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$page = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$toc\+\_\+name = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{TOC}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$templates = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$correct\+\_\+align = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$color = {\ttfamily array(0,0,0)} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Output a Table Of Content Index (TOC) using HTML templates. This method must be called after all Bookmarks were set. Before calling this method you have to open the page using the \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a41c91f0a79fb6623b66866af3c082a7f}{add\+TOCPage()} method. After calling this method you have to call \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ab7698fe46c6756ceef25aad463e6064d}{end\+TOCPage()} to close the TOC page. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
int | null & {\em \$page} & page number where this TOC should be inserted (leave empty for current page). \\
\hline
string & {\em \$toc\+\_\+name} & name to use for TOC bookmark. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$templates} & array of html templates. Use\+: "{}\#\+TOC\+\_\+\+DESCRIPTION\#"{} for bookmark title, "{}\#\+TOC\+\_\+\+PAGE\+\_\+\+NUMBER\#"{} for page number. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$correct\+\_\+align} & if true correct the number alignment (numbers must be in monospaced font like courier and right aligned on LTR, or left aligned on RTL) \\
\hline

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!AddLink@{AddLink}}
\index{AddLink@{AddLink}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AddLink()}{AddLink()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Add\+Link (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Creates a new internal link and returns its identifier. An internal link is a clickable area which directs to another place within the document.~\newline
 The identifier can then be passed to \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a9dec253ab4724f896000e09f4457892b}{Cell()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a7b720385c94078b62062c4bb3f52a97e}{Write()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ab067950824579c1d5f3111b45c9899c2}{Image()} or \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_acb916367a196e0c1593b1f88263c6adc}{Link()}. The destination is defined with \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Link()}.

\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+5 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a01665ab0079fd2137912f76c48cc35c4}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a01665ab0079fd2137912f76c48cc35c4} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!AddPage@{AddPage}}
\index{AddPage@{AddPage}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AddPage()}{AddPage()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Add\+Page (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$orientation = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$format = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$keepmargins = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$tocpage = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Adds a new page to the document. If a page is already present, the \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a2f39533ba0786237090683635ef01c49}{Footer()} method is called first to output the footer (if enabled). Then the page is added, the current position set to the top-\/left corner according to the left and top margins (or top-\/right if in RTL mode), and \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_af476ba4a046025587e6ca04f98918434}{Header()} is called to display the header (if enabled). The origin of the coordinate system is at the top-\/left corner (or top-\/right for RTL) and increasing ordinates go downwards. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$orientation} & page orientation. Possible values are (case insensitive)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item P or PORTRAIT (default)
\item L or LANDSCAPE
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$format} & The format used for pages. It can be either\+: one of the string values specified at get\+Page\+Size\+From\+Format() or an array of parameters specified at \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a31727d77336d2e92a731d4322ed62f46}{set\+Page\+Format()}. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$keepmargins} & if true overwrites the default page margins with the current margins \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$tocpage} & if true set the tocpage state to true (the added page will be used to display Table Of Content).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a6996a8aec4bdcef324b7a6c2046a8e67}{start\+Page()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ad6eb42f89db94fedaf4d77b924ba4ba8}{end\+Page()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a41c91f0a79fb6623b66866af3c082a7f}{add\+TOCPage()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ab7698fe46c6756ceef25aad463e6064d}{end\+TOCPage()}, get\+Page\+Size\+From\+Format(), \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a31727d77336d2e92a731d4322ed62f46}{set\+Page\+Format()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!addPageRegion@{addPageRegion}}
\index{addPageRegion@{addPageRegion}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addPageRegion()}{addPageRegion()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily add\+Page\+Region (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$region }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Add a single no-\/write region on selected page. A no-\/write region is a portion of the page with a rectangular or trapezium shape that will not be covered when writing text or html code. A region is always aligned on the left or right side of the page ad is defined using a vertical segment. You can set multiple regions for the same page. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
array & {\em \$region} & array of a single no-\/write region array\+: (\textquotesingle{}page\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} page number or empy for current page, \textquotesingle{}xt\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} X top, \textquotesingle{}yt\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} Y top, \textquotesingle{}xb\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} X bottom, \textquotesingle{}yb\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} Y bottom, \textquotesingle{}side\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} page side \textquotesingle{}L\textquotesingle{} = left or \textquotesingle{}R\textquotesingle{} = right). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
5.\+9.\+003 (2010-\/10-\/13) 
\end{DoxySince}

Defines a new spot color. It can be expressed in RGB components or gray scale. The method can be called before the first page is created and the value is retained from page to page.

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!addTOC@{addTOC}}
\index{addTOC@{addTOC}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{addTOC()}{addTOC()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily add\+TOC (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$page = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$numbersfont = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$filler = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}.\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$toc\+\_\+name = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{TOC}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$color = {\ttfamily array(0,0,0)} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Output a Table of Content Index (TOC). This method must be called after all Bookmarks were set. Before calling this method you have to open the page using the \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a41c91f0a79fb6623b66866af3c082a7f}{add\+TOCPage()} method. After calling this method you have to call \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ab7698fe46c6756ceef25aad463e6064d}{end\+TOCPage()} to close the TOC page. You can override this method to achieve different styles. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
int | null & {\em \$page} & page number where this TOC should be inserted (leave empty for current page). \\
\hline
string & {\em \$numbersfont} & set the font for page numbers (please use monospaced font for better alignment). \\
\hline
string & {\em \$filler} & string used to fill the space between text and page number. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$toc\+\_\+name} & name to use for TOC bookmark. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Font style for title\+: B = Bold, I = Italic, BI = Bold + Italic. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$color} & RGB color array for bookmark title (values from 0 to 255).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
4.\+5.\+000 (2009-\/01-\/02) 
\end{DoxySince}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!Cell@{Cell}}
\index{Cell@{Cell}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Cell()}{Cell()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Cell (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$txt = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$border = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$ln = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fill = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$link = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$stretch = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$ignore\+\_\+min\+\_\+height = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$calign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{T}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$valign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{M}}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Prints a cell (rectangular area) with optional borders, background color and character string. The upper-\/left corner of the cell corresponds to the current position. The text can be aligned or centered. After the call, the current position moves to the right or to the next line. It is possible to put a link on the text.~\newline
 If automatic page breaking is enabled and the cell goes beyond the limit, a page break is done before outputting. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$w} & Cell width. If 0, the cell extends up to the right margin. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & Cell height. Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$txt} & String to print. Default value\+: empty string. \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$border} & Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell. The value can be a number\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: no border (default)
\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\
\hline
int & {\em \$ln} & Indicates where the current position should go after the call. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: to the right (or left for RTL languages)
\item 1\+: to the beginning of the next line
\item 2\+: below
\end{DoxyItemize}Putting 1 is equivalent to putting 0 and calling \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a61ced26209917509b2315cd23d650b55}{Ln()} just after. Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Allows to center or align the text. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L or empty string\+: left align (default value)
\item C\+: center
\item R\+: right align
\item J\+: justify
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fill} & Indicates if the cell background must be painted (true) or transparent (false). \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$link} & URL or identifier returned by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae5905a6270028a055eb4b7e6f3def713}{Add\+Link()}. \\
\hline
int & {\em \$stretch} & font stretch mode\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0 = disabled
\item 1 = horizontal scaling only if text is larger than cell width
\item 2 = forced horizontal scaling to fit cell width
\item 3 = character spacing only if text is larger than cell width
\item 4 = forced character spacing to fit cell width
\end{DoxyItemize}General font stretching and scaling values will be preserved when possible. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ignore\+\_\+min\+\_\+height} & if true ignore automatic minimum height value. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$calign} & cell vertical alignment relative to the specified Y value. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T \+: cell top
\item C \+: center
\item B \+: cell bottom
\item A \+: font top
\item L \+: font baseline
\item D \+: font bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$valign} & text vertical alignment inside the cell. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T \+: top
\item C \+: center
\item B \+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a9053ddbaa96ec7efc0cc8c725d671f4b}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a9053ddbaa96ec7efc0cc8c725d671f4b} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!checkPageRegions@{checkPageRegions}}
\index{checkPageRegions@{checkPageRegions}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{checkPageRegions()}{checkPageRegions()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily check\+Page\+Regions (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Check page for no-\/write regions and adapt current coordinates and page margins if necessary. A no-\/write region is a portion of the page with a rectangular or trapezium shape that will not be covered when writing text or html code. A region is always aligned on the left or right side of the page ad is defined using a vertical segment. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$h} & height of the text/image/object to print in user units \\
\hline
float & {\em \$x} & current X coordinate in user units \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y} & current Y coordinate in user units \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
float\mbox{[}\mbox{]} array(\$x, \$y) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
5.\+9.\+003 (2010-\/10-\/13) 
\end{DoxySince}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!Circle@{Circle}}
\index{Circle@{Circle}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Circle()}{Circle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Circle (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x0,  }\item[{}]{\$y0,  }\item[{}]{\$r,  }\item[{}]{\$angstr = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$angend = {\ttfamily 360},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$line\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$fill\+\_\+color = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$nc = {\ttfamily 2} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a circle. A circle is formed from n Bezier curves. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$x0} & Abscissa of center point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y0} & Ordinate of center point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$r} & Radius. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$angstr} & Angle start of draw line. Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$angend} & Angle finish of draw line. Default value\+: 360. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Style of rendering. See the get\+Path\+Paint\+Operator() function for more information. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$line\+\_\+style} & \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of circle. Array like for \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Style()}. Default value\+: default line style (empty array). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$fill\+\_\+color} & Fill color. Format\+: array(red, green, blue). Default value\+: default color (empty array). \\
\hline
integer & {\em \$nc} & Number of curves used to draw a 90 degrees portion of circle.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
2.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/01-\/08) 
\end{DoxySince}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!Close@{Close}}
\index{Close@{Close}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Close()}{Close()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Close (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Terminates the PDF document. It is not necessary to call this method explicitly because \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_acd3345feb73cd6addc7ab266fa583e33}{Output()} does it automatically. If the document contains no page, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a01665ab0079fd2137912f76c48cc35c4}{Add\+Page()} is called to prevent from getting an invalid document.

\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!CoonsPatchMesh@{CoonsPatchMesh}}
\index{CoonsPatchMesh@{CoonsPatchMesh}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CoonsPatchMesh()}{CoonsPatchMesh()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Coons\+Patch\+Mesh (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$col1 = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$col2 = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$col3 = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$col4 = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$coords = {\ttfamily array(0.00,0.0,0.33,0.00,0.67,0.00,1.00,0.00,1.00,0.33,1.00,0.67,1.00,1.00,0.67,1.00,0.33,1.00,0.00,1.00,0.00,0.67,0.00,0.33)},  }\item[{}]{\$coords\+\_\+min = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$coords\+\_\+max = {\ttfamily 1},  }\item[{}]{\$antialias = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Paints a coons patch mesh. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$x} & abscissa of the top left corner of the rectangle. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y} & ordinate of the top left corner of the rectangle. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$w} & width of the rectangle. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & height of the rectangle. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$col1} & first color (lower left corner) (RGB components). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$col2} & second color (lower right corner) (RGB components). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$col3} & third color (upper right corner) (RGB components). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$col4} & fourth color (upper left corner) (RGB components). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$coords} & 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item for one patch mesh\+: array(float x1, float y1, .... float x12, float y12)\+: 12 pairs of coordinates (normally from 0 to 1) which specify the Bezier control points that define the patch. First pair is the lower left edge point, next is its right control point (control point 2). Then the other points are defined in the order\+: control point 1, edge point, control point 2 going counter-\/clockwise around the patch. Last (x12, y12) is the first edge point\textquotesingle{}s left control point (control point 1).
\item for two or more patch meshes\+: array\mbox{[}number of patches\mbox{]}\+: arrays with the following keys for each patch\+: f\+: where to put that patch (0 = first patch, 1, 2, 3 = right, top and left of precedent patch -\/ I didn\textquotesingle{}t figure this out completely -\/ just try and error ;-\/) points\+: 12 pairs of coordinates of the Bezier control points as above for the first patch, 8 pairs of coordinates for the following patches, ignoring the coordinates already defined by the precedent patch (I also didn\textquotesingle{}t figure out the order of these -\/ also\+: try and see what\textquotesingle{}s happening) colors\+: must be 4 colors for the first patch, 2 colors for the following patches
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
array & {\em \$coords\+\_\+min} & minimum value used by the coordinates. If a coordinate\textquotesingle{}s value is smaller than this it will be cut to coords\+\_\+min. default\+: 0 \\
\hline
array & {\em \$coords\+\_\+max} & maximum value used by the coordinates. If a coordinate\textquotesingle{}s value is greater than this it will be cut to coords\+\_\+max. default\+: 1 \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$antialias} & A flag indicating whether to filter the shading function to prevent aliasing artifacts. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Andreas W\textbackslash{}\+FCrmser, Nicola Asuni 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
3.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/06-\/09) 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Curve()}{Curve()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Curve (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x0,  }\item[{}]{\$y0,  }\item[{}]{\$x1,  }\item[{}]{\$y1,  }\item[{}]{\$x2,  }\item[{}]{\$y2,  }\item[{}]{\$x3,  }\item[{}]{\$y3,  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$line\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$fill\+\_\+color = {\ttfamily array()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a Bezier curve. The Bezier curve is a tangent to the line between the control points at either end of the curve. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$x0} & Abscissa of start point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y0} & Ordinate of start point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$x1} & Abscissa of control point 1. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y1} & Ordinate of control point 1. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$x2} & Abscissa of control point 2. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y2} & Ordinate of control point 2. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$x3} & Abscissa of end point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y3} & Ordinate of end point. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Style of rendering. See the get\+Path\+Paint\+Operator() function for more information. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$line\+\_\+style} & \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of curve. Array like for \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Style()}. Default value\+: default line style (empty array). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$fill\+\_\+color} & Fill color. Format\+: array(\+GREY) or array(\+R,\+G,\+B) or array(\+C,\+M,\+Y,\+K) or array(\+C,\+M,\+Y,\+K,\+Spot\+Color\+Name). Default value\+: default color (empty array).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Ellipse()}{Ellipse()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ellipse (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x0,  }\item[{}]{\$y0,  }\item[{}]{\$rx,  }\item[{}]{\$ry = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$angle = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$astart = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$afinish = {\ttfamily 360},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$line\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$fill\+\_\+color = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$nc = {\ttfamily 2} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws an ellipse. An ellipse is formed from n Bezier curves. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$x0} & Abscissa of center point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y0} & Ordinate of center point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$rx} & Horizontal radius. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$ry} & Vertical radius (if ry = 0 then is a circle, see \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a29f78edbfd2dfd19e9d6d0b6d329807c}{Circle()}). Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$angle} & Angle oriented (anti-\/clockwise). Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$astart} & Angle start of draw line. Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$afinish} & Angle finish of draw line. Default value\+: 360. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Style of rendering. See the get\+Path\+Paint\+Operator() function for more information. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$line\+\_\+style} & \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of ellipse. Array like for \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Style()}. Default value\+: default line style (empty array). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$fill\+\_\+color} & Fill color. Format\+: array(\+GREY) or array(\+R,\+G,\+B) or array(\+C,\+M,\+Y,\+K) or array(\+C,\+M,\+Y,\+K,\+Spot\+Color\+Name). Default value\+: default color (empty array). \\
\hline
integer & {\em \$nc} & Number of curves used to draw a 90 degrees portion of ellipse. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
2.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/01-\/08)

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!endTemplate@{endTemplate}}
\index{endTemplate@{endTemplate}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{endTemplate()}{endTemplate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily end\+Template (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

End the current XObject Template started with \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_aff989cb6f99329a655b85eabfd60289b}{start\+Template()} and restore the previous graphic state. An XObject Template is a PDF block that is a self-\/contained description of any sequence of graphics objects (including path objects, text objects, and sampled images). An XObject Template may be painted multiple times, either on several pages or at several locations on the same page and produces the same results each time, subject only to the graphics state at the time it is invoked. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}false the XObject Template ID in case of success or false in case of error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
5.\+8.\+017 (2010-\/08-\/24) 
\end{DoxySince}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!GetArrStringWidth@{GetArrStringWidth}}
\index{GetArrStringWidth@{GetArrStringWidth}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetArrStringWidth()}{GetArrStringWidth()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Get\+Arr\+String\+Width (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$sa,  }\item[{}]{\$fontname = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fontstyle = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fontsize = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$getarray = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the string length of an array of chars in user unit or an array of characters widths. A font must be selected.~\newline
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
array & {\em \$sa} & The array of chars whose total length is to be computed \\
\hline
string & {\em \$fontname} & Family font. It can be either a name defined by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a1a0390351695ec7f1a9c01d88d303a87}{Add\+Font()} or one of the standard families. It is also possible to pass an empty string, in that case, the current family is retained. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$fontstyle} & Font style. Possible values are (case insensitive)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item empty string\+: regular
\item B\+: bold
\item I\+: italic
\item U\+: underline
\item D\+: line through
\item O\+: overline
\end{DoxyItemize}or any combination. The default value is regular. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$fontsize} & Font size in points. The default value is the current size. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$getarray} & if true returns an array of characters widths, if false returns the total length. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
float\mbox{[}\mbox{]}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}float total string length or array of characted widths 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
2.\+4.\+000 (2008-\/03-\/06)

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getCellBorder()}{getCellBorder()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily get\+Cell\+Border (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$brd }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}

\begin{DoxyItemize}

\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_ac13b2d3d4487c2b7c045d32b255facbc}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_ac13b2d3d4487c2b7c045d32b255facbc} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!getCellCode@{getCellCode}}
\index{getCellCode@{getCellCode}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getCellCode()}{getCellCode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily get\+Cell\+Code (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$txt = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$border = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$ln = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fill = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$link = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$stretch = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$ignore\+\_\+min\+\_\+height = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$calign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{T}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$valign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{M}}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Returns the PDF string code to print a cell (rectangular area) with optional borders, background color and character string. The upper-\/left corner of the cell corresponds to the current position. The text can be aligned or centered. After the call, the current position moves to the right or to the next line. It is possible to put a link on the text.~\newline
 If automatic page breaking is enabled and the cell goes beyond the limit, a page break is done before outputting. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$w} & Cell width. If 0, the cell extends up to the right margin. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & Cell height. Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$txt} & String to print. Default value\+: empty string. \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$border} & Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell. The value can be a number\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: no border (default)
\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\
\hline
int & {\em \$ln} & Indicates where the current position should go after the call. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: to the right (or left for RTL languages)
\item 1\+: to the beginning of the next line
\item 2\+: below
\end{DoxyItemize}Putting 1 is equivalent to putting 0 and calling \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a61ced26209917509b2315cd23d650b55}{Ln()} just after. Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Allows to center or align the text. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L or empty string\+: left align (default value)
\item C\+: center
\item R\+: right align
\item J\+: justify
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fill} & Indicates if the cell background must be painted (true) or transparent (false). \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$link} & URL or identifier returned by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae5905a6270028a055eb4b7e6f3def713}{Add\+Link()}. \\
\hline
int & {\em \$stretch} & font stretch mode\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0 = disabled
\item 1 = horizontal scaling only if text is larger than cell width
\item 2 = forced horizontal scaling to fit cell width
\item 3 = character spacing only if text is larger than cell width
\item 4 = forced character spacing to fit cell width
\end{DoxyItemize}General font stretching and scaling values will be preserved when possible. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ignore\+\_\+min\+\_\+height} & if true ignore automatic minimum height value. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$calign} & cell vertical alignment relative to the specified Y value. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T \+: cell top
\item C \+: center
\item B \+: cell bottom
\item A \+: font top
\item L \+: font baseline
\item D \+: font bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$valign} & text vertical alignment inside the cell. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T \+: top
\item M \+: middle
\item B \+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string containing cell code
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!getNumLines@{getNumLines}}
\index{getNumLines@{getNumLines}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getNumLines()}{getNumLines()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily get\+Num\+Lines (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$txt,  }\item[{}]{\$w = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$reseth = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$autopadding = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$cellpadding = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$border = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This method return the estimated number of lines for print a simple text string using \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Multicell()} method. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$txt} & String for calculating his height \\
\hline
float & {\em \$w} & Width of cells. If 0, they extend up to the right margin of the page. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$reseth} & if true reset the last cell height (default false). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$autopadding} & if true, uses internal padding and automatically adjust it to account for line width (default true). \\
\hline
array | null & {\em \$cellpadding} & Internal cell padding, if empty uses default cell padding. \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$border} & Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell. The value can be a number\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: no border (default)
\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
float Return the minimal height needed for multicell method for printing the \$txt param. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Alexander Escalona Fern\textbackslash{}\+E1ndez, Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
4.\+5.\+011 
\end{DoxySince}

Returns an array of page dimensions\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}w\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = page width in points
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = height in points
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}wk\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = page width in user units
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}hk\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = page height in user units
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}tm\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = top margin
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}bm\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = bottom margin
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}lm\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = left margin
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}rm\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = right margin
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}pb\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = auto page break
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}or\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = page orientation
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}olm\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = original left margin
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}orm\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = original right margin
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Rotate\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = The number of degrees by which the page shall be rotated clockwise when displayed or printed. The value shall be a multiple of 90.
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}PZ\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = The page\textquotesingle{}s preferred zoom (magnification) factor.
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: the style and duration of the visual transition to use when moving from another page to the given page during a presentation
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Dur\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = The page\textquotesingle{}s display duration (also called its advance timing)\+: the maximum length of time, in seconds, that the page shall be displayed during presentations before the viewer application shall automatically advance to the next page.
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}S\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = transition style \+: Split, Blinds, Box, Wipe, Dissolve, Glitter, R, Fly, Push, Cover, Uncover, Fade
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}D\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = The duration of the transition effect, in seconds.
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Dm\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = (Split and Blinds transition styles only) The dimension in which the specified transition effect shall occur\+: H = Horizontal, V = Vertical. Default value\+: H.
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}M\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = (Split, Box and Fly transition styles only) The direction of motion for the specified transition effect\+: I = Inward from the edges of the page, O = Outward from the center of the page\+Default value\+: I.
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Di\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = (Wipe, Glitter, Fly, Cover, Uncover and Push transition styles only) The direction in which the specified transition effect shall moves, expressed in degrees counterclockwise starting from a left-\/to-\/right direction. If the value is a number, it shall be one of\+: 0 = Left to right, 90 = Bottom to top (Wipe only), 180 = Right to left (Wipe only), 270 = Top to bottom, 315 = Top-\/left to bottom-\/right (Glitter only). If the value is a name, it shall be None, which is relevant only for the Fly transition when the value of SS is not 1.\+0. Default value\+: 0.
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}SS\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = (Fly transition style only) The starting or ending scale at which the changes shall be drawn. If M specifies an inward transition, the scale of the changes drawn shall progress from SS to 1.\+0 over the course of the transition. If M specifies an outward transition, the scale of the changes drawn shall progress from 1.\+0 to SS over the course of the transition. Default\+: 1.\+0. 
\item \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}pagedim\mbox{[}\$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}page\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}B\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = (Fly transition style only) If true, the area that shall be flown in is rectangular and opaque. Default\+: false.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a883fcb745fcd7ba764eaafdc9aefa0c1}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a883fcb745fcd7ba764eaafdc9aefa0c1} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!getStringHeight@{getStringHeight}}
\index{getStringHeight@{getStringHeight}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{getStringHeight()}{getStringHeight()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily get\+String\+Height (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$txt,  }\item[{}]{\$reseth = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$autopadding = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$cellpadding = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$border = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This method return the estimated height needed for printing a simple text string using the \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Multicell()} method. Generally, if you want to know the exact height for a block of content you can use the following alternative technique\+: \begin{DoxyPrecond}{Précondition}
// store current object \$pdf-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a09aabfaecf95a335063d4e237a2c2126}{start\+Transaction()}; // store starting values \$start\+\_\+y = \$pdf-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a6677aaf0484d3b84549d26cd7506b3ca}{Get\+Y()}; \$start\+\_\+page = \$pdf-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a12a549e25239c9219e66322cf6a1be68}{get\+Page()}; // call your printing functions with your parameters // -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ \$pdf-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}Multi\+Cell(\$w=0, \$h=0, \$txt, \$border=1, \$align=\textquotesingle{}L\textquotesingle{}, \$fill=false, \$ln=1, \$x=null, \$y=null, \$reseth=true, \$stretch=0, \$ishtml=false, \$autopadding=true, \$maxh=0); // -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ -\/ // get the new Y \$end\+\_\+y = \$pdf-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a6677aaf0484d3b84549d26cd7506b3ca}{Get\+Y()}; \$end\+\_\+page = \$pdf-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a12a549e25239c9219e66322cf6a1be68}{get\+Page()}; // calculate height \$height = 0; if (\$end\+\_\+page == \$start\+\_\+page) \{ \$height = \$end\+\_\+y -\/ \$start\+\_\+y; \} else \{ for (\$page=\$start\+\_\+page; \$page \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= \$end\+\_\+page; ++\$page) \{ \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}set\+Page(\$page); if (\$page == \$start\+\_\+page) \{ // first page \$height += \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}h -\/ \$start\+\_\+y -\/ \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}b\+Margin; \} elseif (\$page == \$end\+\_\+page) \{ // last page \$height += \$end\+\_\+y -\/ \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}t\+Margin; \} else \{ \$height += \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}h -\/ \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}t\+Margin -\/ \$this-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}b\+Margin; \} \} \} // restore previous object \$pdf = \$pdf-\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ac925ee92dd8f83bc00ca711e58762f73}{rollback\+Transaction()};
\end{DoxyPrecond}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$w} & Width of cells. If 0, they extend up to the right margin of the page. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$txt} & String for calculating his height \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$reseth} & if true reset the last cell height (default false). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$autopadding} & if true, uses internal padding and automatically adjust it to account for line width (default true). \\
\hline
array | null & {\em \$cellpadding} & Internal cell padding, if empty uses default cell padding. \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$border} & Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell. The value can be a number\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: no border (default)
\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
float Return the minimal height needed for multicell method for printing the \$txt param. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni, Alexander Escalona Fern\textbackslash{}\+E1ndez 
\end{DoxyAuthor}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!GetStringWidth@{GetStringWidth}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{GetStringWidth()}{GetStringWidth()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Get\+String\+Width (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$s,  }\item[{}]{\$fontname = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fontstyle = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fontsize = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$getarray = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the length of a string in user unit. A font must be selected.~\newline
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$s} & The string whose length is to be computed \\
\hline
string & {\em \$fontname} & Family font. It can be either a name defined by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a1a0390351695ec7f1a9c01d88d303a87}{Add\+Font()} or one of the standard families. It is also possible to pass an empty string, in that case, the current family is retained. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$fontstyle} & Font style. Possible values are (case insensitive)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item empty string\+: regular
\item B\+: bold
\item I\+: italic
\item U\+: underline
\item D\+: line-\/through
\item O\+: overline
\end{DoxyItemize}or any combination. The default value is regular. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$fontsize} & Font size in points. The default value is the current size. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$getarray} & if true returns an array of characters widths, if false returns the total length. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
float\mbox{[}\mbox{]}\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}float total string length or array of characted widths 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Gradient (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$type,  }\item[{}]{\$coords,  }\item[{}]{\$stops,  }\item[{}]{\$background = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$antialias = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

int & {\em \$type} & type of gradient (1 Function-\/based shading; 2 Axial shading; 3 Radial shading; 4 Free-\/form Gouraud-\/shaded triangle mesh; 5 Lattice-\/form Gouraud-\/shaded triangle mesh; 6 Coons patch mesh; 7 Tensor-\/product patch mesh). (Not all types are currently supported) \\
\hline
array & {\em \$coords} & array of coordinates. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$stops} & array gradient color components\+: color = array of GRAY, RGB or CMYK color components; offset = (0 to 1) represents a location along the gradient vector; exponent = exponent of the exponential interpolation function (default = 1). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$background} & An array of colour components appropriate to the colour space, specifying a single background colour value. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$antialias} & A flag indicating whether to filter the shading function to prevent aliasing artifacts. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
3.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/06-\/09) 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Header()}{Header()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Header (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This method is used to render the page header. It is automatically called by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a01665ab0079fd2137912f76c48cc35c4}{Add\+Page()} and could be overwritten in your own inherited class.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hyphenateText()}{hyphenateText()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily hyphenate\+Text (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$text,  }\item[{}]{\$patterns,  }\item[{}]{\$dictionary = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$leftmin = {\ttfamily 1},  }\item[{}]{\$rightmin = {\ttfamily 2},  }\item[{}]{\$charmin = {\ttfamily 1},  }\item[{}]{\$charmax = {\ttfamily 8} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns text with soft hyphens. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$text} & text to process \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$patterns} & Array of hypenation patterns or a TEX file containing hypenation patterns. TEX patterns can be downloaded from \href{http://www.ctan.org/tex-archive/language/hyph-utf8/tex/generic/hyph-utf8/patterns/}{\texttt{ http\+://www.\+ctan.\+org/tex-\/archive/language/hyph-\/utf8/tex/generic/hyph-\/utf8/patterns/}} \\
\hline
array & {\em \$dictionary} & Array of words to be returned without applying the hyphenation algorithm. \\
\hline
int & {\em \$leftmin} & Minimum number of character to leave on the left of the word without applying the hyphens. \\
\hline
int & {\em \$rightmin} & Minimum number of character to leave on the right of the word without applying the hyphens. \\
\hline
int & {\em \$charmin} & Minimum word length to apply the hyphenation algorithm. \\
\hline
int & {\em \$charmax} & Maximum length of broken piece of word. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_ab067950824579c1d5f3111b45c9899c2}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_ab067950824579c1d5f3111b45c9899c2} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!Image@{Image}}
\index{Image@{Image}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Image()}{Image()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$file,  }\item[{}]{\$x = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$y = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$w = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$h = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$type = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$link = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$resize = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$dpi = {\ttfamily 300},  }\item[{}]{\$palign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$ismask = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$imgmask = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$border = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$fitbox = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$hidden = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$fitonpage = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$alt = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$altimgs = {\ttfamily array()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Puts an image in the page. The upper-\/left corner must be given. The dimensions can be specified in different ways\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item explicit width and height (expressed in user unit) 
\item one explicit dimension, the other being calculated automatically in order to keep the original proportions 
\item no explicit dimension, in which case the image is put at 72 dpi
\end{DoxyItemize}Supported formats are JPEG and PNG images whitout GD library and all images supported by GD\+: GD, GD2, GD2\+PART, GIF, JPEG, PNG, BMP, XBM, XPM; The format can be specified explicitly or inferred from the file extension.~\newline
 It is possible to put a link on the image.~\newline
 Remark\+: if an image is used several times, only one copy will be embedded in the file.~\newline
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$file} & Name of the file containing the image or a \textquotesingle{}@\textquotesingle{} character followed by the image data string. To link an image without embedding it on the document, set an asterisk character before the URL (i.\+e.\+: \textquotesingle{}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}http\+://www.example.\+com/image.jpg\textquotesingle{}). \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$x} & Abscissa of the upper-\/left corner (LTR) or upper-\/right corner (RTL). \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$y} & Ordinate of the upper-\/left corner (LTR) or upper-\/right corner (RTL). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$w} & Width of the image in the page. If not specified or equal to zero, it is automatically calculated. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & Height of the image in the page. If not specified or equal to zero, it is automatically calculated. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$type} & Image format. Possible values are (case insensitive)\+: JPEG and PNG (whitout GD library) and all images supported by GD\+: GD, GD2, GD2\+PART, GIF, JPEG, PNG, BMP, XBM, XPM;. If not specified, the type is inferred from the file extension. \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$link} & URL or identifier returned by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae5905a6270028a055eb4b7e6f3def713}{Add\+Link()}. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Indicates the alignment of the pointer next to image insertion relative to image height. The value can be\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T\+: top-\/right for LTR or top-\/left for RTL
\item M\+: middle-\/right for LTR or middle-\/left for RTL
\item B\+: bottom-\/right for LTR or bottom-\/left for RTL
\item N\+: next line
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$resize} & If true resize (reduce) the image to fit \$w and \$h (requires GD or Image\+Magick library); if false do not resize; if 2 force resize in all cases (upscaling and downscaling). \\
\hline
int & {\em \$dpi} & dot-\/per-\/inch resolution used on resize \\
\hline
string & {\em \$palign} & Allows to center or align the image on the current line. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L \+: left align
\item C \+: center
\item R \+: right align
\item \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} \+: empty string \+: left for LTR or right for RTL
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ismask} & true if this image is a mask, false otherwise \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$imgmask} & image object returned by this function or false \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$border} & Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell. The value can be a number\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: no border (default)
\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$fitbox} & If not false scale image dimensions proportionally to fit within the (\$w, \$h) box. \$fitbox can be true or a 2 characters string indicating the image alignment inside the box. The first character indicate the horizontal alignment (L = left, C = center, R = right) the second character indicate the vertical algnment (T = top, M = middle, B = bottom). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$hidden} & If true do not display the image. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fitonpage} & If true the image is resized to not exceed page dimensions. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$alt} & If true the image will be added as alternative and not directly printed (the ID of the image will be returned). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$altimgs} & Array of alternate images IDs. Each alternative image must be an array with two values\+: an integer representing the image ID (the value returned by the Image method) and a boolean value to indicate if the image is the default for printing. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
mixed\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}false image information
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+1 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a89a2dfa88089460130bd18ff612b3940}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a89a2dfa88089460130bd18ff612b3940} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!ImageEps@{ImageEps}}
\index{ImageEps@{ImageEps}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ImageEps()}{ImageEps()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Image\+Eps (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$file,  }\item[{}]{\$x = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$y = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$w = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$h = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$link = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$use\+Bounding\+Box = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$palign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$border = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$fitonpage = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$fixoutvals = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Embed vector-\/based Adobe Illustrator (AI) or AI-\/compatible EPS files. NOTE\+: EPS is not yet fully implemented, use the \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_acb2d96eca6ade849bcdba74e778f00ca}{set\+Rasterize\+Vector\+Images()} method to enable/disable rasterization of vector images using Image\+Magick library. Only vector drawing is supported, not text or bitmap. Although the script was successfully tested with various AI format versions, best results are probably achieved with files that were exported in the AI3 format (tested with Illustrator CS2, Freehand MX and Photoshop CS2). 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$file} & Name of the file containing the image or a \textquotesingle{}@\textquotesingle{} character followed by the EPS/\+AI data string. \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$x} & Abscissa of the upper-\/left corner. \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$y} & Ordinate of the upper-\/left corner. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$w} & Width of the image in the page. If not specified or equal to zero, it is automatically calculated. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & Height of the image in the page. If not specified or equal to zero, it is automatically calculated. \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$link} & URL or identifier returned by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae5905a6270028a055eb4b7e6f3def713}{Add\+Link()}. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$use\+Bounding\+Box} & specifies whether to position the bounding box (true) or the complete canvas (false) at location (x,y). Default value is true. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Indicates the alignment of the pointer next to image insertion relative to image height. The value can be\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T\+: top-\/right for LTR or top-\/left for RTL
\item M\+: middle-\/right for LTR or middle-\/left for RTL
\item B\+: bottom-\/right for LTR or bottom-\/left for RTL
\item N\+: next line
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$palign} & Allows to center or align the image on the current line. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L \+: left align
\item C \+: center
\item R \+: right align
\item \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} \+: empty string \+: left for LTR or right for RTL
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$border} & Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell. The value can be a number\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: no border (default)
\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fitonpage} & if true the image is resized to not exceed page dimensions. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fixoutvals} & if true remove values outside the bounding box. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Valentin Schmidt, Nicola Asuni 
\end{DoxyAuthor}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ImagePngAlpha()}{ImagePngAlpha()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Image\+Png\+Alpha (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$file,  }\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$wpx,  }\item[{}]{\$hpx,  }\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$type,  }\item[{}]{\$link,  }\item[{}]{\$align,  }\item[{}]{\$resize,  }\item[{}]{\$dpi,  }\item[{}]{\$palign,  }\item[{}]{\$filehash = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

\hline
float & {\em \$h} & Height of the image in the page. If not specified or equal to zero, it is automatically calculated. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$type} & Image format. Possible values are (case insensitive)\+: JPEG and PNG (whitout GD library) and all images supported by GD\+: GD, GD2, GD2\+PART, GIF, JPEG, PNG, BMP, XBM, XPM;. If not specified, the type is inferred from the file extension. \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$link} & URL or identifier returned by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae5905a6270028a055eb4b7e6f3def713}{Add\+Link()}. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Indicates the alignment of the pointer next to image insertion relative to image height. The value can be\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T\+: top-\/right for LTR or top-\/left for RTL
\item M\+: middle-\/right for LTR or middle-\/left for RTL
\item B\+: bottom-\/right for LTR or bottom-\/left for RTL

\item \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} \+: empty string \+: left for LTR or right for RTL

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!ImageSVG@{ImageSVG}}
\index{ImageSVG@{ImageSVG}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ImageSVG()}{ImageSVG()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Image\+SVG (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$file,  }\item[{}]{\$x = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$y = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$w = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$h = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$link = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$palign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$border = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$fitonpage = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Embedd a Scalable Vector Graphics (SVG) image. NOTE\+: SVG standard is not yet fully implemented, use the \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_acb2d96eca6ade849bcdba74e778f00ca}{set\+Rasterize\+Vector\+Images()} method to enable/disable rasterization of vector images using Image\+Magick library. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$file} & Name of the SVG file or a \textquotesingle{}@\textquotesingle{} character followed by the SVG data string. \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$x} & Abscissa of the upper-\/left corner. \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$y} & Ordinate of the upper-\/left corner. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$w} & Width of the image in the page. If not specified or equal to zero, it is automatically calculated. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & Height of the image in the page. If not specified or equal to zero, it is automatically calculated. \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$link} & URL or identifier returned by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae5905a6270028a055eb4b7e6f3def713}{Add\+Link()}. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Indicates the alignment of the pointer next to image insertion relative to image height. The value can be\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T\+: top-\/right for LTR or top-\/left for RTL
\item M\+: middle-\/right for LTR or middle-\/left for RTL
\item B\+: bottom-\/right for LTR or bottom-\/left for RTL
\item N\+: next line
\end{DoxyItemize}If the alignment is an empty string, then the pointer will be restored on the starting SVG position. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$palign} & Allows to center or align the image on the current line. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L \+: left align
\item C \+: center
\item R \+: right align
\item \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} \+: empty string \+: left for LTR or right for RTL
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$border} & Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell. The value can be a number\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: no border (default)
\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fitonpage} & if true the image is resized to not exceed page dimensions. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
5.\+0.\+000 (2010-\/05-\/02) 
\end{DoxySince}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Linear\+Gradient (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$col1 = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$col2 = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$coords = {\ttfamily array(0,0,1,0)} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

array & {\em \$col1} & first color (Grayscale, RGB or CMYK components). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$col2} & second color (Grayscale, RGB or CMYK components). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$coords} & array of the form (x1, y1, x2, y2) which defines the gradient vector (see linear\+\_\+gradient\+\_\+coords.\+jpg). The default value is from left to right (x1=0, y1=0, x2=1, y2=0). \\
