\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!Link@{Link}}
\index{Link@{Link}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Link()}{Link()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{class_link}{Link}} (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$link,  }\item[{}]{\$spaces = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Puts a link on a rectangular area of the page. Text or image links are generally put via \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a9dec253ab4724f896000e09f4457892b}{Cell()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a7b720385c94078b62062c4bb3f52a97e}{Write()} or \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ab067950824579c1d5f3111b45c9899c2}{Image()}, but this method can be useful for instance to define a clickable area inside an image. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$x} & Abscissa of the upper-\/left corner of the rectangle \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y} & Ordinate of the upper-\/left corner of the rectangle \\
\hline
float & {\em \$w} & Width of the rectangle \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & Height of the rectangle \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$link} & URL or identifier returned by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae5905a6270028a055eb4b7e6f3def713}{Add\+Link()} \\
\hline
int & {\em \$spaces} & number of spaces on the text to link\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+5 
\end{DoxySince}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!Ln@{Ln}}
\index{Ln@{Ln}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Ln()}{Ln()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Ln (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$h = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$cell = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Performs a line break. The current abscissa goes back to the left margin and the ordinate increases by the amount passed in parameter. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float | null & {\em \$h} & The height of the break. By default, the value equals the height of the last printed cell. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$cell} & if true add the current left (or right o for RTL) padding to the X coordinate\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a5410e2ff685477ddf40e20aa9ae442aa}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a5410e2ff685477ddf40e20aa9ae442aa} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!MultiCell@{MultiCell}}
\index{MultiCell@{MultiCell}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MultiCell()}{MultiCell()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Multi\+Cell (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$txt,  }\item[{}]{\$border = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{J}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fill = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$ln = {\ttfamily 1},  }\item[{}]{\$x = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$y = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$reseth = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$stretch = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$ishtml = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$autopadding = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$maxh = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$valign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{T}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fitcell = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This method allows printing text with line breaks. They can be automatic (as soon as the text reaches the right border of the cell) or explicit (via the ~\newline
 character). As many cells as necessary are output, one below the other.~\newline
 Text can be aligned, centered or justified. The cell block can be framed and the background painted. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$w} & Width of cells. If 0, they extend up to the right margin of the page. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & Cell minimum height. The cell extends automatically if needed. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$txt} & String to print \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$border} & Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell. The value can be a number\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: no border (default)
\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Allows to center or align the text. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L or empty string\+: left align
\item C\+: center
\item R\+: right align
\item J\+: justification (default value when \$ishtml=false)
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fill} & Indicates if the cell background must be painted (true) or transparent (false). \\
\hline
int & {\em \$ln} & Indicates where the current position should go after the call. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: to the right
\item 1\+: to the beginning of the next line \mbox{[}DEFAULT\mbox{]}
\item 2\+: below
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$x} & x position in user units \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$y} & y position in user units \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$reseth} & if true reset the last cell height (default true). \\
\hline
int & {\em \$stretch} & font stretch mode\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0 = disabled
\item 1 = horizontal scaling only if text is larger than cell width
\item 2 = forced horizontal scaling to fit cell width
\item 3 = character spacing only if text is larger than cell width
\item 4 = forced character spacing to fit cell width
\end{DoxyItemize}General font stretching and scaling values will be preserved when possible. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ishtml} & INTERNAL USE ONLY -- set to true if \$txt is HTML content (default = false). Never set this parameter to true, use instead \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_aa5f289d5c4341e38727e9c8ab625fb10}{write\+HTMLCell()} or \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a59fedc90bb3a10d07cd476e7d282b2db}{write\+HTML()} methods. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$autopadding} & if true, uses internal padding and automatically adjust it to account for line width. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$maxh} & maximum height. It should be \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}= \$h and less then remaining space to the bottom of the page, or 0 for disable this feature. This feature works only when \$ishtml=false. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$valign} & Vertical alignment of text (requires \$maxh = \$h \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0). Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T\+: TOP
\item M\+: middle
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}. This feature works only when \$ishtml=false and the cell must fit in a single page. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fitcell} & if true attempt to fit all the text within the cell by reducing the font size (do not work in HTML mode). \$maxh must be greater than 0 and equal to \$h. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
int Return the number of cells or 1 for html mode.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+3 
\end{DoxySince}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Font()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Draw\+Color()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Fill\+Color()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Text\+Color()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Width()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a9dec253ab4724f896000e09f4457892b}{Cell()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a7b720385c94078b62062c4bb3f52a97e}{Write()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Auto\+Page\+Break()}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_acd3345feb73cd6addc7ab266fa583e33}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_acd3345feb73cd6addc7ab266fa583e33} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!Output@{Output}}
\index{Output@{Output}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Output()}{Output()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Output (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$name = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}doc.pdf\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$dest = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{I}}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Send the document to a given destination\+: string, local file or browser. In the last case, the plug-\/in may be used (if present) or a download ("{}\+Save as"{} dialog box) may be forced.~\newline
 The method first calls \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a2fd4e06444aa4ace4cab6d6950ba2bb2}{Close()} if necessary to terminate the document. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$name} & The name of the file when saved \\
\hline
string & {\em \$dest} & Destination where to send the document. It can take one of the following values\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item I\+: send the file inline to the browser (default). The plug-\/in is used if available. The name given by name is used when one selects the "{}\+Save as"{} option on the link generating the PDF.
\item D\+: send to the browser and force a file download with the name given by name.
\item F\+: save to a local server file with the name given by name.
\item S\+: return the document as a string (name is ignored).
\item FI\+: equivalent to F + I option
\item FD\+: equivalent to F + D option
\item E\+: return the document as base64 mime multi-\/part email attachment (RFC 2045)
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!PieSector@{PieSector}}
\index{PieSector@{PieSector}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{PieSector()}{PieSector()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Pie\+Sector (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$xc,  }\item[{}]{\$yc,  }\item[{}]{\$r,  }\item[{}]{\$a,  }\item[{}]{\$b,  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{FD}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$cw = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$o = {\ttfamily 90} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draw the sector of a circle. It can be used for instance to render pie charts. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$xc} & abscissa of the center. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$yc} & ordinate of the center. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$r} & radius. \\

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a3cac90754d4d713376b4ce30a4f16e72}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a3cac90754d4d713376b4ce30a4f16e72} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!printTemplate@{printTemplate}}
\index{printTemplate@{printTemplate}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{printTemplate()}{printTemplate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily print\+Template (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$id,  }\item[{}]{\$x = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$y = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$w = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$h = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$palign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fitonpage = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Print an XObject Template. You can print an XObject Template inside the currently opened Template. An XObject Template is a PDF block that is a self-\/contained description of any sequence of graphics objects (including path objects, text objects, and sampled images). An XObject Template may be painted multiple times, either on several pages or at several locations on the same page and produces the same results each time, subject only to the graphics state at the time it is invoked. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$id} & The ID of XObject Template to print. \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$x} & X position in user units (empty string = current x position) \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$y} & Y position in user units (empty string = current y position) \\
\hline
float & {\em \$w} & Width in user units (zero = remaining page width) \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & Height in user units (zero = remaining page height) \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Indicates the alignment of the pointer next to template insertion relative to template height. The value can be\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T\+: top-\/right for LTR or top-\/left for RTL
\item M\+: middle-\/right for LTR or middle-\/left for RTL
\item B\+: bottom-\/right for LTR or bottom-\/left for RTL
\item N\+: next line
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$palign} & Allows to center or align the template on the current line. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L \+: left align
\item C \+: center
\item R \+: right align
\item \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} \+: empty string \+: left for LTR or right for RTL
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fitonpage} & If true the template is resized to not exceed page dimensions. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
5.\+8.\+017 (2010-\/08-\/24) 
\end{DoxySince}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Radial\+Gradient (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$col1 = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$col2 = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$coords = {\ttfamily array(0.5,0.5,0.5,0.5,1)} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Paints a radial colour gradient. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$x} & abscissa of the top left corner of the rectangle. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y} & ordinate of the top left corner of the rectangle. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$w} & width of the rectangle. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & height of the rectangle. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$col1} & first color (Grayscale, RGB or CMYK components). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$col2} & second color (Grayscale, RGB or CMYK components). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$coords} & array of the form (fx, fy, cx, cy, r) where (fx, fy) is the starting point of the gradient with color1, (cx, cy) is the center of the circle with color2, and r is the radius of the circle (see radial\+\_\+gradient\+\_\+coords.\+jpg). (fx, fy) should be inside the circle, otherwise some areas will not be defined. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$border\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$fill\+\_\+color = {\ttfamily array()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Style of rendering. See the get\+Path\+Paint\+Operator() function for more information. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$border\+\_\+style} & Border style of rectangle. Array with keys among the following\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}

\end{DoxyItemize}If a key is not present or is null, the correspondent border is not drawn. Default value\+: default line style (empty array). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$fill\+\_\+color} & Fill color. Format\+: array(\+GREY) or array(\+R,\+G,\+B) or array(\+C,\+M,\+Y,\+K) or array(\+C,\+M,\+Y,\+K,\+Spot\+Color\+Name). Default value\+: default color (empty array).\\

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!RegularPolygon@{RegularPolygon}}
\index{RegularPolygon@{RegularPolygon}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{RegularPolygon()}{RegularPolygon()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Regular\+Polygon (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x0,  }\item[{}]{\$y0,  }\item[{}]{\$r,  }\item[{}]{\$ns,  }\item[{}]{\$angle = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$draw\+\_\+circle = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$line\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$fill\+\_\+color = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$circle\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$circle\+\_\+out\+Line\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$circle\+\_\+fill\+\_\+color = {\ttfamily array()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a regular polygon. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$x0} & Abscissa of center point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y0} & Ordinate of center point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$r} & Radius of inscribed circle. \\
\hline
integer & {\em \$ns} & Number of sides. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$angle} & Angle oriented (anti-\/clockwise). Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$draw\+\_\+circle} & Draw inscribed circle or not. Default value\+: false. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Style of rendering. See the get\+Path\+Paint\+Operator() function for more information. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$line\+\_\+style} & \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of polygon sides. Array with keys among the following\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item all\+: \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of all sides. Array like for \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Style()}. 
\item 0 to (\$ns -\/ 1)\+: \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of each side. Array like for \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Style()}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}If a key is not present or is null, not draws the side. Default value is default line style (empty array). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$fill\+\_\+color} & Fill color. Format\+: array(red, green, blue). Default value\+: default color (empty array). \\
\hline
string & {\em \$circle\+\_\+style} & Style of rendering of inscribed circle (if draws). Possible values are\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item D or empty string\+: Draw (default). 
\item F\+: Fill. 
\item DF or FD\+: Draw and fill. 
\item CNZ\+: Clipping mode (using the even-\/odd rule to determine which regions lie inside the clipping path). 
\item CEO\+: Clipping mode (using the nonzero winding number rule to determine which regions lie inside the clipping path). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
array & {\em \$circle\+\_\+out\+Line\+\_\+style} & \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of inscribed circle (if draws). Array like for \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Style()}. Default value\+: default line style (empty array). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$circle\+\_\+fill\+\_\+color} & Fill color of inscribed circle (if draws). Format\+: array(red, green, blue). Default value\+: default color (empty array).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

2.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/01-\/08)

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!RoundedRect@{RoundedRect}}
\index{RoundedRect@{RoundedRect}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{RoundedRect()}{RoundedRect()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Rounded\+Rect (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$r,  }\item[{}]{\$round\+\_\+corner = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}1111\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$border\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$fill\+\_\+color = {\ttfamily array()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a rounded rectangle. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$x} & Abscissa of upper-\/left corner. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y} & Ordinate of upper-\/left corner. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$w} & Width. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$h} & Height. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$r} & the radius of the circle used to round off the corners of the rectangle. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$round\+\_\+corner} & Draws rounded corner or not. String with a 0 (not rounded i-\/corner) or 1 (rounded i-\/corner) in i-\/position. Positions are, in order and begin to 0\+: top right, bottom right, bottom left and top left. Default value\+: all rounded corner ("{}1111"{}). \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Style of rendering. See the get\+Path\+Paint\+Operator() function for more information. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$border\+\_\+style} & Border style of rectangle. Array like for \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Style()}. Default value\+: default line style (empty array). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$fill\+\_\+color} & Fill color. Format\+: array(\+GREY) or array(\+R,\+G,\+B) or array(\+C,\+M,\+Y,\+K) or array(\+C,\+M,\+Y,\+K,\+Spot\+Color\+Name). Default value\+: default color (empty array).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
2.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/01-\/08) 
\end{DoxySince}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Auto\+Page\+Break (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$auto,  }\item[{}]{\$margin = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enables or disables the automatic page breaking mode. When enabling, the second parameter is the distance from the bottom of the page that defines the triggering limit. By default, the mode is on and the margin is 2 cm. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
boolean & {\em \$auto} & Boolean indicating if mode should be on or off. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$margin} & Distance from the bottom of the page.\\

\hline
int & {\em \$level} & Bookmark level (minimum value is 0). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y} & Y position in user units of the bookmark on the selected page (default = -\/1 = current position; 0 = page start;). \\
\hline
int | string & {\em \$page} & Target page number (leave empty for current page). If you prefix a page number with the \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} character, then this page will not be changed when adding/deleting/moving pages. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Font style\+: B = Bold, I = Italic, BI = Bold + Italic. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$color} & RGB color array (values from 0 to 255). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$x} & X position in user units of the bookmark on the selected page (default = -\/1 = current position;). \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$link} & URL, or numerical link ID, or named destination (\# character followed by the destination name), or embedded file (\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} character followed by the file name). \\
\hline

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setColorArray@{setColorArray}}
\index{setColorArray@{setColorArray}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setColorArray()}{setColorArray()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Color\+Array (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$type,  }\item[{}]{\$color,  }\item[{}]{\$ret = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the color array for the specified type (\textquotesingle{}draw\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}fill\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}text\textquotesingle{}). It can be expressed in RGB, CMYK or GRAY SCALE components. The method can be called before the first page is created and the value is retained from page to page. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$type} & Type of object affected by this color\+: (\textquotesingle{}draw\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}fill\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}text\textquotesingle{}). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$color} & Array of colors (1=gray, 3=RGB, 4=CMYK or 5=spotcolor=CMYK+name values). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ret} & If true do not send the PDF command. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string The PDF command or empty string.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
3.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/06-\/11) 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_ab231450a00f9697c427ceb390361fa08}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_ab231450a00f9697c427ceb390361fa08} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setCompression@{setCompression}}
\index{setCompression@{setCompression}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setCompression()}{setCompression()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Compression (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$compress = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Activates or deactivates page compression. When activated, the internal representation of each page is compressed, which leads to a compression ratio of about 2 for the resulting document. Compression is on by default. Note\+: the Zlib extension is required for this feature. If not present, compression will be turned off. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
boolean & {\em \$compress} & Boolean indicating if compression must be enabled.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+4 
\end{DoxySince}
Voici le graphe des appelants de cette fonction \+:
\nopagebreak
\begin{figure}[H]

{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Destination (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$name,  }\item[{}]{\$y = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{}]{\$page = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$x = {\ttfamily -\/1} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$name} & Destination name. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y} & Y position in user units of the destiantion on the selected page (default = -\/1 = current position; 0 = page start;). \\
\hline
int | string & {\em \$page} & Target page number (leave empty for current page). If you prefix a page number with the \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} character, then this page will not be changed when adding/deleting/moving pages. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$x} & X position in user units of the destiantion on the selected page (default = -\/1 = current position;). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}false Stripped named destination identifier or false in case of error.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setDisplayMode@{setDisplayMode}}
\index{setDisplayMode@{setDisplayMode}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setDisplayMode()}{setDisplayMode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Display\+Mode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$zoom,  }\item[{}]{\$layout = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Single\+Page}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$mode = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Use\+None}}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Defines the way the document is to be displayed by the viewer. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
mixed & {\em \$zoom} & The zoom to use. It can be one of the following string values or a number indicating the zooming factor to use. 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item fullpage\+: displays the entire page on screen 
\item fullwidth\+: uses maximum width of window
\item real\+: uses real size (equivalent to 100\% zoom)
\item default\+: uses viewer default mode
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$layout} & The page layout. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Single\+Page Display one page at a time
\item One\+Column Display the pages in one column
\item Two\+Column\+Left Display the pages in two columns, with odd-\/numbered pages on the left
\item Two\+Column\+Right Display the pages in two columns, with odd-\/numbered pages on the right
\item Two\+Page\+Left (PDF 1.\+5) Display the pages two at a time, with odd-\/numbered pages on the left
\item Two\+Page\+Right (PDF 1.\+5) Display the pages two at a time, with odd-\/numbered pages on the right
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$mode} & A name object specifying how the document should be displayed when opened\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Use\+None Neither document outline nor thumbnail images visible
\item Use\+Outlines \doxylink{class_document}{Document} outline visible
\item Use\+Thumbs Thumbnail images visible
\item Full\+Screen Full-\/screen mode, with no menu bar, window controls, or any other window visible
\item Use\+OC (PDF 1.\+5) Optional content group panel visible
\item Use\+Attachments (PDF 1.\+6) Attachments panel visible
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+2 
\end{DoxySince}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Draw\+Color (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$col1 = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$col2 = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{}]{\$col3 = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{}]{\$col4 = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{}]{\$ret = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$name = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Defines the color used for all drawing operations (lines, rectangles and cell borders). It can be expressed in RGB components or gray scale. The method can be called before the first page is created and the value is retained from page to page. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$col1} & GRAY level for single color, or Red color for RGB (0-\/255), or CYAN color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$col2} & GREEN color for RGB (0-\/255), or MAGENTA color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$col3} & BLUE color for RGB (0-\/255), or YELLOW color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$col4} & KEY (BLACK) color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ret} & If true do not send the command. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$name} & spot color name (if any) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string the PDF command
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Extra\+XMP (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$xmp }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set additional XMP data to be added on the default XMP data just before the end of "{}x\+:xmpmeta"{} tag. IMPORTANT\+: This data is added as-\/is without controls, so you have to validate your data before using this method! 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setFillColor@{setFillColor}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setFillColor()}{setFillColor()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Fill\+Color (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$col1 = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$col2 = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{}]{\$col3 = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{}]{\$col4 = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{}]{\$ret = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$name = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Defines the color used for all filling operations (filled rectangles and cell backgrounds). It can be expressed in RGB components or gray scale. The method can be called before the first page is created and the value is retained from page to page. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$col1} & GRAY level for single color, or Red color for RGB (0-\/255), or CYAN color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$col2} & GREEN color for RGB (0-\/255), or MAGENTA color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$col3} & BLUE color for RGB (0-\/255), or YELLOW color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$col4} & KEY (BLACK) color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ret} & If true do not send the command. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$name} & Spot color name (if any). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string The PDF command.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+3 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a72c67d12759f8b67b9085ff0a274ee62}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a72c67d12759f8b67b9085ff0a274ee62} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setFont@{setFont}}
\index{setFont@{setFont}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setFont()}{setFont()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Font (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$family,  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$size = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$fontfile = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$subset = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{default}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$out = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Sets the font used to print character strings. The font can be either a standard one or a font added via the \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a1a0390351695ec7f1a9c01d88d303a87}{Add\+Font()} method. Standard fonts use Windows encoding cp1252 (Western Europe). The method can be called before the first page is created and the font is retained from page to page. If you just wish to change the current font size, it is simpler to call \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Font\+Size()}. Note\+: for the standard fonts, the font metric files must be accessible. There are three possibilities for this\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item They are in the current directory (the one where the running script lies)
\item They are in one of the directories defined by the include\+\_\+path parameter
\item They are in the directory defined by the K\+\_\+\+PATH\+\_\+\+FONTS constant
\end{DoxyItemize}~\newline
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$family} & Family font. It can be either a name defined by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a1a0390351695ec7f1a9c01d88d303a87}{Add\+Font()} or one of the standard Type1 families (case insensitive)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item times (Times-\/\+Roman)
\item timesb (Times-\/\+Bold)
\item timesi (Times-\/\+Italic)
\item timesbi (Times-\/\+Bold\+Italic)
\item helvetica (Helvetica)
\item helveticab (Helvetica-\/\+Bold)
\item helveticai (Helvetica-\/\+Oblique)
\item helveticabi (Helvetica-\/\+Bold\+Oblique)
\item courier (Courier)
\item courierb (Courier-\/\+Bold)
\item courieri (Courier-\/\+Oblique)
\item courierbi (Courier-\/\+Bold\+Oblique)
\item symbol (Symbol)
\item zapfdingbats (Zapf\+Dingbats)
\end{DoxyItemize}It is also possible to pass an empty string. In that case, the current family is retained. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Font style. Possible values are (case insensitive)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item empty string\+: regular
\item B\+: bold
\item I\+: italic
\item U\+: underline
\item D\+: line through
\item O\+: overline
\end{DoxyItemize}or any combination. The default value is regular. Bold and italic styles do not apply to Symbol and Zapf\+Dingbats basic fonts or other fonts when not defined. \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$size} & Font size in points. The default value is the current size. If no size has been specified since the beginning of the document, the value taken is 12 \\
\hline
string & {\em \$fontfile} & The font definition file. By default, the name is built from the family and style, in lower case with no spaces. \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$subset} & if true embedd only a subset of the font (stores only the information related to the used characters); if false embedd full font; if \textquotesingle{}default\textquotesingle{} uses the default value set using \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a8b5e171af1fa013b2cda7ec6005af7c0}{set\+Font\+Subsetting()}. This option is valid only for True\+Type\+Unicode fonts. If you want to enable users to change the document, set this parameter to false. If you subset the font, the person who receives your PDF would need to have your same font in order to make changes to your PDF. The file size of the PDF would also be smaller because you are embedding only part of a font. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$out} & if true output the font size command, otherwise only set the font properties. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{setHtmlVSpace@{setHtmlVSpace}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setHtmlVSpace()}{setHtmlVSpace()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Html\+VSpace (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$tagvs }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the vertical spaces for HTML tags. The array must have the following structure (example)\+: \$tagvs = array(\textquotesingle{}h1\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0 =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}n\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2), 1 =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}h\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 1.\+3, \textquotesingle{}n\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 1))); The first array level contains the tag names, the second level contains 0 for opening tags or 1 for closing tags, the third level contains the vertical space unit (h) and the number spaces to add (n). If the h parameter is not specified, default values are used. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
array & {\em \$tagvs} & array of tags and relative vertical spaces.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
4.\+2.\+001 (2008-\/10-\/30) 
\end{DoxySince}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setLineStyle@{setLineStyle}}
\index{setLineStyle@{setLineStyle}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setLineStyle()}{setLineStyle()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Line\+Style (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$style,  }\item[{}]{\$ret = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set line style. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
array & {\em \$style} & \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style. Array with keys among the following\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item width (float)\+: Width of the line in user units. 
\item cap (string)\+: Type of cap to put on the line. Possible values are\+: butt, round, square. The difference between "{}square"{} and "{}butt"{} is that "{}square"{} projects a flat end past the end of the line. 
\item join (string)\+: Type of join. Possible values are\+: miter, round, bevel. 
\item dash (mixed)\+: Dash pattern. Is 0 (without dash) or string with series of length values, which are the lengths of the on and off dashes. For example\+: "{}2"{} represents 2 on, 2 off, 2 on, 2 off, ...; "{}2,1"{} is 2 on, 1 off, 2 on, 1 off, ... 
\item phase (integer)\+: Modifier on the dash pattern which is used to shift the point at which the pattern starts. 
\item color (array)\+: Draw color. Format\+: array(\+GREY) or array(\+R,\+G,\+B) or array(\+C,\+M,\+Y,\+K) or array(\+C,\+M,\+Y,\+K,\+Spot\+Color\+Name). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ret} & if true do not send the command. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string the PDF command
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
2.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/01-\/08) 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a31727d77336d2e92a731d4322ed62f46}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a31727d77336d2e92a731d4322ed62f46} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setPageFormat@{setPageFormat}}
\index{setPageFormat@{setPageFormat}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setPageFormat()}{setPageFormat()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Page\+Format (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$format,  }\item[{}]{\$orientation = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{P}}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

\doxylink{class_change}{Change} the format of the current page 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
mixed & {\em \$format} & The format used for pages. It can be either\+: one of the string values specified at get\+Page\+Size\+From\+Format() documentation or an array of two numbers (width, height) or an array containing the following measures and options\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}format\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} = page format name (one of the above); 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Rotate\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: The number of degrees by which the page shall be rotated clockwise when displayed or printed. The value shall be a multiple of 90. 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}PZ\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: The page\textquotesingle{}s preferred zoom (magnification) factor. 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Media\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: the boundaries of the physical medium on which the page shall be displayed or printed\+: 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Media\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}llx\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: lower-\/left x coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Media\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}lly\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: lower-\/left y coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Media\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}urx\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: upper-\/right x coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Media\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}ury\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: upper-\/right y coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Crop\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: the visible region of default user space\+: 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Crop\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}llx\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: lower-\/left x coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Crop\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}lly\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: lower-\/left y coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Crop\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}urx\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: upper-\/right x coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Crop\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}ury\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: upper-\/right y coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Bleed\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: the region to which the contents of the page shall be clipped when output in a production environment\+: 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Bleed\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}llx\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: lower-\/left x coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Bleed\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}lly\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: lower-\/left y coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Bleed\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}urx\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: upper-\/right x coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Bleed\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}ury\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: upper-\/right y coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Trim\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: the intended dimensions of the finished page after trimming\+: 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Trim\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}llx\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: lower-\/left x coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Trim\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}lly\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: lower-\/left y coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Trim\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}urx\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: upper-\/right x coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Trim\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}ury\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: upper-\/right y coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Art\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: the extent of the page\textquotesingle{}s meaningful content\+: 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Art\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}llx\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: lower-\/left x coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Art\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}lly\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: lower-\/left y coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Art\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}urx\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: upper-\/right x coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Art\+Box\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}ury\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: upper-\/right y coordinate 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Box\+Color\+Info\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+:specify the colours and other visual characteristics that should be used in displaying guidelines on the screen for each of the possible page boundaries other than the Media\+Box\+: 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Box\+Color\+Info\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}BOXTYPE\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}C\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: an array of three numbers in the range 0-\/255, representing the components in the Device\+RGB colour space. 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Box\+Color\+Info\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}BOXTYPE\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}W\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: the guideline width in default user units 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Box\+Color\+Info\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}BOXTYPE\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}S\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: the guideline style\+: S = Solid; D = Dashed 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Box\+Color\+Info\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}BOXTYPE\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}D\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: dash array defining a pattern of dashes and gaps to be used in drawing dashed guidelines 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: the style and duration of the visual transition to use when moving from another page to the given page during a presentation 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Dur\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: The page\textquotesingle{}s display duration (also called its advance timing)\+: the maximum length of time, in seconds, that the page shall be displayed during presentations before the viewer application shall automatically advance to the next page. 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}S\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: transition style \+: Split, Blinds, Box, Wipe, Dissolve, Glitter, R, Fly, Push, Cover, Uncover, Fade 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}D\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: The duration of the transition effect, in seconds. 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Dm\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: (Split and Blinds transition styles only) The dimension in which the specified transition effect shall occur\+: H = Horizontal, V = Vertical. Default value\+: H. 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}M\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: (Split, Box and Fly transition styles only) The direction of motion for the specified transition effect\+: I = Inward from the edges of the page, O = Outward from the center of the page\+Default value\+: I. 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}Di\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: (Wipe, Glitter, Fly, Cover, Uncover and Push transition styles only) The direction in which the specified transition effect shall moves, expressed in degrees counterclockwise starting from a left-\/to-\/right direction. If the value is a number, it shall be one of\+: 0 = Left to right, 90 = Bottom to top (Wipe only), 180 = Right to left (Wipe only), 270 = Top to bottom, 315 = Top-\/left to bottom-\/right (Glitter only). If the value is a name, it shall be None, which is relevant only for the Fly transition when the value of SS is not 1.\+0. Default value\+: 0. 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}SS\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: (Fly transition style only) The starting or ending scale at which the changes shall be drawn. If M specifies an inward transition, the scale of the changes drawn shall progress from SS to 1.\+0 over the course of the transition. If M specifies an outward transition, the scale of the changes drawn shall progress from 1.\+0 to SS over the course of the transition. Default\+: 1.\+0. 
\item \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}trans\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}B\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} \+: (Fly transition style only) If true, the area that shall be flown in is rectangular and opaque. Default\+: false. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$orientation} & page orientation. Possible values are (case insensitive)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item P or Portrait (default) 
\item L or Landscape 
\item \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} (empty string) for automatic orientation 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
3.\+0.\+015 (2008-\/06-\/06) 
\end{DoxySince}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setPageMark@{setPageMark}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setPageMark()}{setPageMark()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Page\+Mark (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set start-\/writing mark on current page stream used to put borders and fills. Borders and fills are always created after content and inserted on the position marked by this method. This function must be called after calling \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ab067950824579c1d5f3111b45c9899c2}{Image()} function for a background image. Background images must be always inserted before calling \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Multicell()} or \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Write\+HTMLCell()} or \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Write\+HTML()} functions.

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setPageRegions@{setPageRegions}}
\index{setPageRegions@{setPageRegions}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setPageRegions()}{setPageRegions()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Page\+Regions (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$regions = {\ttfamily array()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set no-\/write regions on page. A no-\/write region is a portion of the page with a rectangular or trapezium shape that will not be covered when writing text or html code. A region is always aligned on the left or right side of the page ad is defined using a vertical segment. You can set multiple regions for the same page. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
array & {\em \$regions} & array of no-\/write regions. For each region you can define an array as follow\+: (\textquotesingle{}page\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} page number or empy for current page, \textquotesingle{}xt\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} X top, \textquotesingle{}yt\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} Y top, \textquotesingle{}xb\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} X bottom, \textquotesingle{}yb\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} Y bottom, \textquotesingle{}side\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} page side \textquotesingle{}L\textquotesingle{} = left or \textquotesingle{}R\textquotesingle{} = right). Omit this parameter to remove all regions. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
5.\+9.\+003 (2010-\/10-\/13) 
\end{DoxySince}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Page\+Unit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$unit }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the units of measure for the document. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$unit} & \doxylink{class_user}{User} measure unit. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item pt\+: point
\item mm\+: millimeter (default)
\item cm\+: centimeter
\item in\+: inch
\end{DoxyItemize}~\newline
A point equals 1/72 of inch, that is to say about 0.\+35 mm (an inch being 2.\+54 cm). This is a very common unit in typography; font sizes are expressed in that unit.\\

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae80b24dd5c38e2db9473cc404ad822c6}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae80b24dd5c38e2db9473cc404ad822c6} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setProtection@{setProtection}}
\index{setProtection@{setProtection}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setProtection()}{setProtection()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Protection (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$permissions = {\ttfamily array(\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{print}}\textquotesingle{},~\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{modify}}\textquotesingle{},~\textquotesingle{}copy\textquotesingle{},~\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{annot}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{forms}}\textquotesingle{},~\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{fill}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{forms}}\textquotesingle{},~\textquotesingle{}extract\textquotesingle{},~\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{assemble}}\textquotesingle{},~\textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{print}}-\/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{high}}\textquotesingle{})},  }\item[{}]{\$user\+\_\+pass = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$owner\+\_\+pass = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$mode = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$pubkeys = {\ttfamily null} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set document protection Remark\+: the protection against modification is for people who have the full Acrobat product. If you don\textquotesingle{}t set any password, the document will open as usual. If you set a user password, the PDF viewer will ask for it before displaying the document. The master password, if different from the user one, can be used to get full access. Note\+: protecting a document requires to encrypt it, which increases the processing time a lot. This can cause a PHP time-\/out in some cases, especially if the document contains images or fonts. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
array & {\em \$permissions} & the set of permissions (specify the ones you want to block)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item print \+: Print the document;
\item modify \+: Modify the contents of the document by operations other than those controlled by \textquotesingle{}fill-\/forms\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}extract\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}assemble\textquotesingle{};
\item copy \+: Copy or otherwise extract text and graphics from the document;
\item annot-\/forms \+: Add or modify text annotations, fill in interactive form fields, and, if \textquotesingle{}modify\textquotesingle{} is also set, create or modify interactive form fields (including signature fields);
\item fill-\/forms \+: Fill in existing interactive form fields (including signature fields), even if \textquotesingle{}annot-\/forms\textquotesingle{} is not specified;
\item extract \+: Extract text and graphics (in support of accessibility to users with disabilities or for other purposes);
\item assemble \+: Assemble the document (insert, rotate, or delete pages and create bookmarks or thumbnail images), even if \textquotesingle{}modify\textquotesingle{} is not set;
\item print-\/high \+: Print the document to a representation from which a faithful digital copy of the PDF content could be generated. When this is not set, printing is limited to a low-\/level representation of the appearance, possibly of degraded quality.
\item owner \+: (inverted logic -\/ only for public-\/key) when set permits change of encryption and enables all other permissions.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$user\+\_\+pass} & user password. Empty by default. \\
\hline
string | null & {\em \$owner\+\_\+pass} & owner password. If not specified, a random value is used. \\
\hline
int & {\em \$mode} & encryption strength\+: 0 = RC4 40 bit; 1 = RC4 128 bit; 2 = AES 128 bit; 3 = AES 256 bit. \\
\hline
array | null & {\em \$pubkeys} & array of recipients containing public-\/key certificates (\textquotesingle{}c\textquotesingle{}) and permissions (\textquotesingle{}p\textquotesingle{}). For example\+: array(array(\textquotesingle{}c\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}\href{file://../examples/data/cert/tcpdf.crt'}{\texttt{ file\+://../examples/data/cert/tcpdf.\+crt\textquotesingle{}}}, \textquotesingle{}p\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}print\textquotesingle{})))\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
2.\+0.\+000 (2008-\/01-\/02) 
\end{DoxySince}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni 
\end{DoxyAuthor}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_ac611358ba44b0c578f5e0ee167671fd2}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_ac611358ba44b0c578f5e0ee167671fd2} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setSignature@{setSignature}}
\index{setSignature@{setSignature}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setSignature()}{setSignature()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Signature (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$signing\+\_\+cert = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$private\+\_\+key = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$private\+\_\+key\+\_\+password = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$extracerts = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$cert\+\_\+type = {\ttfamily 2},  }\item[{}]{\$info = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$approval = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enable document signature (requires the Open\+SSL Library). The digital signature improve document authenticity and integrity and allows o enable extra features on Acrobat Reader. To create self-\/signed signature\+: openssl req -\/x509 -\/nodes -\/days 365000 -\/newkey rsa\+:1024 -\/keyout tcpdf.\+crt -\/out tcpdf.\+crt To export crt to p12\+: openssl pkcs12 -\/export -\/in tcpdf.\+crt -\/out tcpdf.\+p12 To convert pfx certificate to pem\+: openssl pkcs12 -\/in tcpdf.\+pfx -\/out tcpdf.\+crt -\/nodes 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
mixed & {\em \$signing\+\_\+cert} & signing certificate (string or filename prefixed with \textquotesingle{}\href{file://'}{\texttt{ file\+://\textquotesingle{}}}) \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$private\+\_\+key} & private key (string or filename prefixed with \textquotesingle{}\href{file://'}{\texttt{ file\+://\textquotesingle{}}}) \\
\hline
string & {\em \$private\+\_\+key\+\_\+password} & password \\
\hline
string & {\em \$extracerts} & specifies the name of a file containing a bunch of extra certificates to include in the signature which can for example be used to help the recipient to verify the certificate that you used. \\
\hline
int & {\em \$cert\+\_\+type} & The access permissions granted for this document. Valid values shall be\+: 1 = No changes to the document shall be permitted; any change to the document shall invalidate the signature; 2 = Permitted changes shall be filling in forms, instantiating page templates, and signing; other changes shall invalidate the signature; 3 = Permitted changes shall be the same as for 2, as well as annotation creation, deletion, and modification; other changes shall invalidate the signature. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$info} & array of option information\+: Name, \doxylink{class_location}{Location}, Reason, Contact\+Info. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$approval} & Enable approval signature eg. for PDF incremental update\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
4.\+6.\+005 (2009-\/04-\/24) 
\end{DoxySince}
Voici le graphe d\textquotesingle{}appel pour cette fonction \+:
\nopagebreak
\begin{figure}[H]

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a2cac0bb8c60ef7d7c9c19221e62dee7e}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a2cac0bb8c60ef7d7c9c19221e62dee7e} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setSpacesRE@{setSpacesRE}}
\index{setSpacesRE@{setSpacesRE}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setSpacesRE()}{setSpacesRE()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Spaces\+RE (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$re = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}/\mbox{[}\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}\textbackslash{}S\textbackslash{}xa0\mbox{]}/\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set regular expression to detect withespaces or word separators. The pattern delimiter must be the forward-\/slash character "{}/"{}. Some example patterns are\+: 
\begin{DoxyPre}
Non-\/Unicode or missing PCRE unicode support: "{}/[^\(\backslash\)S\(\backslash\)xa0]/"{}
Unicode and PCRE unicode support: "{}/(?!\(\backslash\)xa0)[\(\backslash\)s\(\backslash\)p\{Z\}]/u"{}
Unicode and PCRE unicode support in Chinese mode: "{}/(?!\(\backslash\)xa0)[\(\backslash\)s\(\backslash\)p\{Z\}\(\backslash\)p\{Lo\}]/u"{}
if PCRE unicode support is turned ON ("{}\(\backslash\)P"{} is the negate class of "{}\(\backslash\)p"{}):
     \(\backslash\)s     : any whitespace character
     {\ttfamily }\{Z\}  : any separator
     {\ttfamily }\{Lo\} : Unicode letter or ideograph that does not have lowercase and uppercase variants. Is used to chunk chinese words.
     \(\backslash\)xa0   : Unicode Character 'NO-\/BREAK SPACE' (U+00A0)
\end{DoxyPre}
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$re} & regular expression (leave empty for default).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
4.\+6.\+016 (2009-\/06-\/15) 
\end{DoxySince}

Defines the color used for text. It can be expressed in RGB components or gray scale. The method can be called before the first page is created and the value is retained from page to page. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}

float & {\em \$col2} & GREEN color for RGB (0-\/255), or MAGENTA color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$col3} & BLUE color for RGB (0-\/255), or YELLOW color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$col4} & KEY (BLACK) color for CMYK (0-\/100). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ret} & If true do not send the command. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$name} & Spot color name (if any). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

string Empty string.

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setTimeStamp@{setTimeStamp}}
\index{setTimeStamp@{setTimeStamp}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setTimeStamp()}{setTimeStamp()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Time\+Stamp (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$tsa\+\_\+host = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$tsa\+\_\+username = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$tsa\+\_\+password = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$tsa\+\_\+cert = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enable document timestamping (requires the Open\+SSL Library). The trusted timestamping improve document security that means that no one should be able to change the document once it has been recorded. Use with digital signature only! 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$tsa\+\_\+host} & Time Stamping Authority (TSA) server (prefixed with \textquotesingle{}\href{https://'}{\texttt{ https\+://\textquotesingle{}}}) \\
\hline
string & {\em \$tsa\+\_\+username} & Specifies the username for TSA authorization (optional) OR specifies the TSA authorization PEM file (see\+: example\+\_\+66.\+php, optional) \\
\hline
string & {\em \$tsa\+\_\+password} & Specifies the password for TSA authorization (optional) \\
\hline
string & {\em \$tsa\+\_\+cert} & Specifies the location of TSA certificate for authorization (optional for c\+URL)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Richard Stockinger 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
6.\+0.\+090 (2014-\/06-\/16) 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setUserRights()}{setUserRights()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+User\+Rights (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$enable = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$document = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Full\+Save}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$annots = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}/Create/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Delete}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Modify}}/Copy/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Import}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Export}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$form = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}/Add/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Delete}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Fill\+In}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Import}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Export}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Submit\+Standalone}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Spawn\+Template}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$signature = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Modify}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$ef = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}/Create/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Delete}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Modify}}/\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Import}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$formex = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set \doxylink{class_user}{User}\textquotesingle{}s Rights for PDF Reader WARNING\+: This is experimental and currently do not work. Check the PDF Reference 8.\+7.\+1 Transform Methods, Table 8.\+105 Entries in the UR transform parameters dictionary 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
boolean & {\em \$enable} & if true enable user\textquotesingle{}s rights on PDF reader \\
\hline
string & {\em \$document} & Names specifying additional document-\/wide usage rights for the document. The only defined value is "{}/\+Full\+Save"{}, which permits a user to save the document along with modified form and/or annotation data. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$annots} & Names specifying additional annotation-\/related usage rights for the document. Valid names in PDF 1.\+5 and later are /\+Create/\+Delete/\+Modify/\+Copy/\+Import/\+Export, which permit the user to perform the named operation on annotations. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$form} & Names specifying additional form-\/field-\/related usage rights for the document. Valid names are\+: /\+Add/\+Delete/\+Fill\+In/\+Import/\+Export/\+Submit\+Standalone/\+Spawn\+Template \\
\hline
string & {\em \$signature} & Names specifying additional signature-\/related usage rights for the document. The only defined value is /\+Modify, which permits a user to apply a digital signature to an existing signature form field or clear a signed signature form field. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$ef} & Names specifying additional usage rights for named embedded files in the document. Valid names are /\+Create/\+Delete/\+Modify/\+Import, which permit the user to perform the named operation on named embedded files Names specifying additional embedded-\/files-\/related usage rights for the document. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$formex} & Names specifying additional form-\/field-\/related usage rights. The only valid name is Barcode\+Plaintext, which permits text form field data to be encoded as a plaintext two-\/dimensional barcode.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!setViewerPreferences@{setViewerPreferences}}
\index{setViewerPreferences@{setViewerPreferences}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{setViewerPreferences()}{setViewerPreferences()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily set\+Viewer\+Preferences (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$preferences }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Set the viewer preferences dictionary controlling the way the document is to be presented on the screen or in print. (see Section 8.\+1 of PDF reference, "{}\+Viewer Preferences"{}). 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Hide\+Toolbar boolean (Optional) A flag specifying whether to hide the viewer application\textquotesingle{}s tool bars when the document is active. Default value\+: false.
\item Hide\+Menubar boolean (Optional) A flag specifying whether to hide the viewer application\textquotesingle{}s menu bar when the document is active. Default value\+: false.
\item Hide\+Window\+UI boolean (Optional) A flag specifying whether to hide user interface elements in the document\textquotesingle{}s window (such as scroll bars and navigation controls), leaving only the document\textquotesingle{}s contents displayed. Default value\+: false.
\item Fit\+Window boolean (Optional) A flag specifying whether to resize the document\textquotesingle{}s window to fit the size of the first displayed page. Default value\+: false.
\item Center\+Window boolean (Optional) A flag specifying whether to position the document\textquotesingle{}s window in the center of the screen. Default value\+: false.
\item Display\+Doc\+Title boolean (Optional; PDF 1.\+4) A flag specifying whether the window\textquotesingle{}s title bar should display the document title taken from the Title entry of the document information dictionary (see Section 10.\+2.\+1, "{}\+Document Information Dictionary"{}). If false, the title bar should instead display the name of the PDF file containing the document. Default value\+: false.
\item Non\+Full\+Screen\+Page\+Mode name (Optional) The document\textquotesingle{}s page mode, specifying how to display the document on exiting full-\/screen mode\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Use\+None Neither document outline nor thumbnail images visible
\item Use\+Outlines \doxylink{class_document}{Document} outline visible
\item Use\+Thumbs Thumbnail images visible
\item Use\+OC Optional content group panel visible
\end{DoxyItemize}This entry is meaningful only if the value of the Page\+Mode entry in the catalog dictionary (see Section 3.\+6.\+1, "{}\+Document Catalog"{}) is Full\+Screen; it is ignored otherwise. Default value\+: Use\+None.
\item View\+Area name (Optional; PDF 1.\+4) The name of the page boundary representing the area of a page to be displayed when viewing the document on the screen. Valid values are (see Section 10.\+10.\+1, "{}\+Page Boundaries"{}).\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Media\+Box
\item Crop\+Box (default)
\item Bleed\+Box
\item Trim\+Box
\item Art\+Box
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item View\+Clip name (Optional; PDF 1.\+4) The name of the page boundary to which the contents of a page are to be clipped when viewing the document on the screen. Valid values are (see Section 10.\+10.\+1, "{}\+Page Boundaries"{}).\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Media\+Box
\item Crop\+Box (default)
\item Bleed\+Box
\item Trim\+Box
\item Art\+Box
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Print\+Area name (Optional; PDF 1.\+4) The name of the page boundary representing the area of a page to be rendered when printing the document. Valid values are (see Section 10.\+10.\+1, "{}\+Page Boundaries"{}).\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Media\+Box
\item Crop\+Box (default)
\item Bleed\+Box
\item Trim\+Box
\item Art\+Box
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Print\+Clip name (Optional; PDF 1.\+4) The name of the page boundary to which the contents of a page are to be clipped when printing the document. Valid values are (see Section 10.\+10.\+1, "{}\+Page Boundaries"{}).\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Media\+Box
\item Crop\+Box (default)
\item Bleed\+Box
\item Trim\+Box
\item Art\+Box
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Print\+Scaling name (Optional; PDF 1.\+6) The page scaling option to be selected when a print dialog is displayed for this document. Valid values are\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item None, which indicates that the print dialog should reflect no page scaling
\item App\+Default (default), which indicates that applications should use the current print scaling
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Duplex name (Optional; PDF 1.\+7) The paper handling option to use when printing the file from the print dialog. The following values are valid\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Simplex -\/ Print single-\/sided
\item Duplex\+Flip\+Short\+Edge -\/ Duplex and flip on the short edge of the sheet
\item Duplex\+Flip\+Long\+Edge -\/ Duplex and flip on the long edge of the sheet
\end{DoxyItemize}Default value\+: none
\item Pick\+Tray\+By\+PDFSize boolean (Optional; PDF 1.\+7) A flag specifying whether the PDF page size is used to select the input paper tray. This setting influences only the preset values used to populate the print dialog presented by a PDF viewer application. If Pick\+Tray\+By\+PDFSize is true, the check box in the print dialog associated with input paper tray is checked. Note\+: This setting has no effect on Mac OS systems, which do not provide the ability to pick the input tray by size.
\item Print\+Page\+Range array (Optional; PDF 1.\+7) The page numbers used to initialize the print dialog box when the file is printed. The first page of the PDF file is denoted by 1. Each pair consists of the first and last pages in the sub-\/range. An odd number of integers causes this entry to be ignored. Negative numbers cause the entire array to be ignored. Default value\+: as defined by PDF viewer application
\item Num\+Copies integer (Optional; PDF 1.\+7) The number of copies to be printed when the print dialog is opened for this file. Supported values are the integers 2 through 5. Values outside this range are ignored. Default value\+: as defined by PDF viewer application, but typically 1
\end{DoxyItemize}
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
array & {\em \$preferences} & array of options. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
3.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/06-\/09) 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{StarPolygon()}{StarPolygon()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Star\+Polygon (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x0,  }\item[{}]{\$y0,  }\item[{}]{\$r,  }\item[{}]{\$nv,  }\item[{}]{\$ng,  }\item[{}]{\$angle = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$draw\+\_\+circle = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$line\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$fill\+\_\+color = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$circle\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$circle\+\_\+out\+Line\+\_\+style = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$circle\+\_\+fill\+\_\+color = {\ttfamily array()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Draws a star polygon 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$x0} & Abscissa of center point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y0} & Ordinate of center point. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$r} & Radius of inscribed circle. \\
\hline
integer & {\em \$nv} & Number of vertices. \\
\hline
integer & {\em \$ng} & Number of gap (if (\$ng \% \$nv = 1) then is a regular polygon). \\
\hline
float & {\em \$angle} & Angle oriented (anti-\/clockwise). Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$draw\+\_\+circle} & Draw inscribed circle or not. Default value is false. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Style of rendering. See the get\+Path\+Paint\+Operator() function for more information. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$line\+\_\+style} & \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of polygon sides. Array with keys among the following\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item all\+: \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of all sides. Array like for \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Style()}. 
\item 0 to (n -\/ 1)\+: \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of each side. Array like for \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Style()}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}If a key is not present or is null, not draws the side. Default value is default line style (empty array). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$fill\+\_\+color} & Fill color. Format\+: array(red, green, blue). Default value\+: default color (empty array). \\
\hline
string & {\em \$circle\+\_\+style} & Style of rendering of inscribed circle (if draws). Possible values are\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item D or empty string\+: Draw (default). 
\item F\+: Fill. 
\item DF or FD\+: Draw and fill. 
\item CNZ\+: Clipping mode (using the even-\/odd rule to determine which regions lie inside the clipping path). 
\item CEO\+: Clipping mode (using the nonzero winding number rule to determine which regions lie inside the clipping path). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
array & {\em \$circle\+\_\+out\+Line\+\_\+style} & \doxylink{class_line}{Line} style of inscribed circle (if draws). Array like for \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Set\+Line\+Style()}. Default value\+: default line style (empty array). \\
\hline
array & {\em \$circle\+\_\+fill\+\_\+color} & Fill color of inscribed circle (if draws). Format\+: array(red, green, blue). Default value\+: default color (empty array).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily start\+Page (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$orientation = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$format = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$tocpage = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Starts a new page to the document. The page must be closed using the \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ad6eb42f89db94fedaf4d77b924ba4ba8}{end\+Page()} function. The origin of the coordinate system is at the top-\/left corner and increasing ordinates go downwards. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$orientation} & page orientation. Possible values are (case insensitive)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item P or PORTRAIT (default)
\item L or LANDSCAPE
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$format} & The format used for pages. It can be either\+: one of the string values specified at get\+Page\+Size\+From\+Format() or an array of parameters specified at \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a31727d77336d2e92a731d4322ed62f46}{set\+Page\+Format()}. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$tocpage} & if true the page is designated to contain the Table-\/\+Of-\/\+Content. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

4.\+2.\+010 (2008-\/11-\/14)

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!startSVGElementHandler@{startSVGElementHandler}}
\index{startSVGElementHandler@{startSVGElementHandler}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startSVGElementHandler()}{startSVGElementHandler()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily start\+SVGElement\+Handler (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$parser,  }\item[{}]{\$name,  }\item[{}]{\$attribs,  }\item[{}]{\$ctm = {\ttfamily array()} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Sets the opening SVG element handler function for the \doxylink{class_x_m_l}{XML} parser. (\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} TO BE COMPLETED \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}) 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
resource | string & {\em \$parser} & The first parameter, parser, is a reference to the \doxylink{class_x_m_l}{XML} parser calling the handler. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$name} & The second parameter, name, contains the name of the element for which this handler is called. If case-\/folding is in effect for this parser, the element name will be in uppercase letters. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$attribs} & The third parameter, attribs, contains an associative array with the element\textquotesingle{}s attributes (if any). The keys of this array are the attribute names, the values are the attribute values. \doxylink{class_attribute}{Attribute} names are case-\/folded on the same criteria as element names. \doxylink{class_attribute}{Attribute} values are not case-\/folded. The original order of the attributes can be retrieved by walking through attribs the normal way, using each(). The first key in the array was the first attribute, and so on. \\
\hline
array & {\em \$ctm} & tranformation matrix for clipping mode (starting transformation matrix). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
5.\+0.\+000 (2010-\/05-\/02) 
\end{DoxySince}
