\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_aff989cb6f99329a655b85eabfd60289b}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_aff989cb6f99329a655b85eabfd60289b} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!startTemplate@{startTemplate}}
\index{startTemplate@{startTemplate}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{startTemplate()}{startTemplate()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily start\+Template (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$w = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$h = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$group = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Start a new XObject Template. An XObject Template is a PDF block that is a self-\/contained description of any sequence of graphics objects (including path objects, text objects, and sampled images). An XObject Template may be painted multiple times, either on several pages or at several locations on the same page and produces the same results each time, subject only to the graphics state at the time it is invoked. Note\+: X,Y coordinates will be reset to 0,0. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
int & {\em \$w} & Template width in user units (empty string or zero = page width less margins). \\
\hline
int & {\em \$h} & Template height in user units (empty string or zero = page height less margins). \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$group} & Set transparency group. Can be a boolean value or an array specifying optional parameters\+: \textquotesingle{}CS\textquotesingle{} (solour space name), \textquotesingle{}I\textquotesingle{} (boolean flag to indicate isolated group) and \textquotesingle{}K\textquotesingle{} (boolean flag to indicate knockout group). \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
string\texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}false the XObject Template ID in case of success or false in case of error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
5.\+8.\+017 (2010-\/08-\/24) 
\end{DoxySince}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}

\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!StartTransform@{StartTransform}}
\index{StartTransform@{StartTransform}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{StartTransform()}{StartTransform()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Start\+Transform (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Starts a 2D tranformation saving current graphic state. This function must be called before scaling, mirroring, translation, rotation and skewing. Use \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a423f35a24bc8b05df61de7deb99796fb}{Start\+Transform()} before, and \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a98166f6cbfa514755ca54720054849c5}{Stop\+Transform()} after the transformations to restore the normal behavior.

\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
2.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/01-\/07) 
\end{DoxySince}

\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_a98166f6cbfa514755ca54720054849c5}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_a98166f6cbfa514755ca54720054849c5} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!StopTransform@{StopTransform}}
\index{StopTransform@{StopTransform}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{StopTransform()}{StopTransform()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Stop\+Transform (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Stops a 2D tranformation restoring previous graphic state. This function must be called after scaling, mirroring, translation, rotation and skewing. Use \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a423f35a24bc8b05df61de7deb99796fb}{Start\+Transform()} before, and \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a98166f6cbfa514755ca54720054849c5}{Stop\+Transform()} after the transformations to restore the normal behavior.

\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
2.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/01-\/07) 
\end{DoxySince}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a423f35a24bc8b05df61de7deb99796fb}{Start\+Transform()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a98166f6cbfa514755ca54720054849c5}{Stop\+Transform()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!SVGPath@{SVGPath}}
\index{SVGPath@{SVGPath}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SVGPath()}{SVGPath()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily SVGPath (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$d,  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [protected]}}

Draws an SVG path 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$d} & attribute d of the path SVG element \\
\hline
string & {\em \$style} & Style of rendering. Possible values are\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item D or empty string\+: Draw (default). 
\item F\+: Fill. 
\item F\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+: Fill using the even-\/odd rule to determine which regions lie inside the clipping path. 
\item DF or FD\+: Draw and fill. 
\item DF\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} or FD\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\+: Draw and fill using the even-\/odd rule to determine which regions lie inside the clipping path. 
\item CNZ\+: Clipping mode (using the even-\/odd rule to determine which regions lie inside the clipping path). 
\item CEO\+: Clipping mode (using the nonzero winding number rule to determine which regions lie inside the clipping path). 
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
array of container box measures (x, y, w, h) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
5.\+0.\+000 (2010-\/05-\/02) 
\end{DoxySince}

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!Text@{Text}}
\index{Text@{Text}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Text()}{Text()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Text (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$txt,  }\item[{}]{\$fstroke = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$fclip = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$ffill = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$border = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$ln = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fill = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$link = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$stretch = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$ignore\+\_\+min\+\_\+height = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$calign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{T}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$valign = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\mbox{\hyperlink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{M}}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$rtloff = {\ttfamily false} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Prints a text cell at the specified position. This method allows to place a string precisely on the page. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$x} & Abscissa of the cell origin \\
\hline
float & {\em \$y} & Ordinate of the cell origin \\
\hline
string & {\em \$txt} & String to print \\
\hline
int & {\em \$fstroke} & outline size in user units (0 = disable) \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fclip} & if true activate clipping mode (you must call \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a423f35a24bc8b05df61de7deb99796fb}{Start\+Transform()} before this function and \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a98166f6cbfa514755ca54720054849c5}{Stop\+Transform()} to stop the clipping tranformation). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ffill} & if true fills the text \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$border} & Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell. The value can be a number\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: no border (default)
\item 1\+: frame
\end{DoxyItemize}or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order)\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+: left
\item T\+: top
\item R\+: right
\item B\+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}or an array of line styles for each border group -\/ for example\+: array(\textquotesingle{}LTRB\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(\textquotesingle{}width\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2, \textquotesingle{}cap\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}butt\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}join\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} \textquotesingle{}miter\textquotesingle{}, \textquotesingle{}dash\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 0, \textquotesingle{}color\textquotesingle{} =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} array(0, 0, 0))) \\
\hline
int & {\em \$ln} & Indicates where the current position should go after the call. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0\+: to the right (or left for RTL languages)
\item 1\+: to the beginning of the next line
\item 2\+: below
\end{DoxyItemize}Putting 1 is equivalent to putting 0 and calling \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a61ced26209917509b2315cd23d650b55}{Ln()} just after. Default value\+: 0. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Allows to center or align the text. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L or empty string\+: left align (default value)
\item C\+: center
\item R\+: right align
\item J\+: justify
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fill} & Indicates if the cell background must be painted (true) or transparent (false). \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$link} & URL or identifier returned by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae5905a6270028a055eb4b7e6f3def713}{Add\+Link()}. \\
\hline
int & {\em \$stretch} & font stretch mode\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0 = disabled
\item 1 = horizontal scaling only if text is larger than cell width
\item 2 = forced horizontal scaling to fit cell width
\item 3 = character spacing only if text is larger than cell width
\item 4 = forced character spacing to fit cell width
\end{DoxyItemize}General font stretching and scaling values will be preserved when possible. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ignore\+\_\+min\+\_\+height} & if true ignore automatic minimum height value. \\
\hline
string & {\em \$calign} & cell vertical alignment relative to the specified Y value. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T \+: cell top
\item A \+: font top
\item L \+: font baseline
\item D \+: font bottom
\item B \+: cell bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$valign} & text vertical alignment inside the cell. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T \+: top
\item C \+: center
\item B \+: bottom
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$rtloff} & if true uses the page top-\/left corner as origin of axis for \$x and \$y initial position.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Write()}{Write()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Write (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$txt,  }\item[{}]{\$link = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$fill = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$ln = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$stretch = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$firstline = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$firstblock = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$maxh = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$wadj = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$margin = {\ttfamily null} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This method prints text from the current position.~\newline
 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
float & {\em \$h} & \doxylink{class_line}{Line} height \\
\hline
string & {\em \$txt} & String to print \\
\hline
mixed & {\em \$link} & URL or identifier returned by \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_ae5905a6270028a055eb4b7e6f3def713}{Add\+Link()} \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fill} & Indicates if the cell background must be painted (true) or transparent (false). \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Allows to center or align the text. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L or empty string\+: left align (default value)
\item C\+: center
\item R\+: right align
\item J\+: justify
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ln} & if true set cursor at the bottom of the line, otherwise set cursor at the top of the line. \\
\hline
int & {\em \$stretch} & font stretch mode\+: 
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0 = disabled
\item 1 = horizontal scaling only if text is larger than cell width
\item 2 = forced horizontal scaling to fit cell width
\item 3 = character spacing only if text is larger than cell width
\item 4 = forced character spacing to fit cell width
\end{DoxyItemize}General font stretching and scaling values will be preserved when possible. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$firstline} & if true prints only the first line and return the remaining string. \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$firstblock} & if true the string is the starting of a line. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$maxh} & maximum height. It should be \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}= \$h and less then remaining space to the bottom of the page, or 0 for disable this feature. \\
\hline
float & {\em \$wadj} & first line width will be reduced by this amount (used in HTML mode). \\
\hline
array | null & {\em \$margin} & margin array of the parent container \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Renvoie}
mixed Return the number of cells or the remaining string if \$firstline = true.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
1.\+5 
\end{DoxySince}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{write1DBarcode()}{write1DBarcode()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily write1\+DBarcode (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$code,  }\item[{}]{\$type,  }\item[{}]{\$x = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$y = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$w = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$h = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$xres = {\ttfamily null},  }\item[{}]{\$style = {\ttfamily array()},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Print a Linear Barcode. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$code} & code to print \\
\hline
string & {\em \$type} & type of barcode (see \doxylink{tcpdf__barcodes__1d_8php}{tcpdf\+\_\+barcodes\+\_\+1d.\+php} for supported formats). \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$x} & x position in user units (null = current x position) \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$y} & y position in user units (null = current y position) \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$w} & width in user units (null = remaining page width) \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$h} & height in user units (null = remaining page height) \\
\hline
float | null & {\em \$xres} & width of the smallest bar in user units (null = default value = 0.\+4mm) \\
\hline
array & {\em \$style} & array of options\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item boolean \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}border\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} if true prints a border 
\item int \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}padding\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} padding to leave around the barcode in user units (set to \textquotesingle{}auto\textquotesingle{} for automatic padding) 
\item int \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}hpadding\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} horizontal padding in user units (set to \textquotesingle{}auto\textquotesingle{} for automatic padding) 
\item int \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}vpadding\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} vertical padding in user units (set to \textquotesingle{}auto\textquotesingle{} for automatic padding) 
\item array \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}fgcolor\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} color array for bars and text 
\item mixed \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}bgcolor\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} color array for background (set to false for transparent) 
\item boolean \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}text\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} if true prints text below the barcode 
\item string \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}label\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} override default label 
\item string \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}font\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} font name for text
\item int \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}fontsize\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} font size for text 
\item int \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}stretchtext\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]}\+: 0 = disabled; 1 = horizontal scaling only if necessary; 2 = forced horizontal scaling; 3 = character spacing only if necessary; 4 = forced character spacing. 
\item string \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}position\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} horizontal position of the containing barcode cell on the page\+: L = left margin; C = center; R = right margin. 
\item string \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}align\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} horizontal position of the barcode on the containing rectangle\+: L = left; C = center; R = right. 
\item string \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}stretch\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} if true stretch the barcode to best fit the available width, otherwise uses \$xres resolution for a single bar. 
\item string \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}fitwidth\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} if true reduce the width to fit the barcode width + padding. When this option is enabled the \textquotesingle{}stretch\textquotesingle{} option is automatically disabled. 
\item string \$style\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}cellfitalign\textquotesingle{}\mbox{]} this option works only when \textquotesingle{}fitwidth\textquotesingle{} is true and \textquotesingle{}position\textquotesingle{} is unset or empty. Set the horizontal position of the containing barcode cell inside the specified rectangle\+: L = left; C = center; R = right.
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Indicates the alignment of the pointer next to barcode insertion relative to barcode height. The value can be\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item T\+: top-\/right for LTR or top-\/left for RTL
\item M\+: middle-\/right for LTR or middle-\/left for RTL
\item B\+: bottom-\/right for LTR or bottom-\/left for RTL
\item N\+: next line
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Nicola Asuni 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
\begin{DoxySince}{Depuis}
3.\+1.\+000 (2008-\/06-\/09) 
\end{DoxySince}

\item N\+: next line

\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!writeHTML@{writeHTML}}
\index{writeHTML@{writeHTML}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{writeHTML()}{writeHTML()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily write\+HTML (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$html,  }\item[{}]{\$ln = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$fill = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$reseth = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$cell = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Allows to preserve some HTML formatting (limited support).~\newline
 IMPORTANT\+: The HTML must be well formatted -\/ try to clean-\/up it using an application like HTML-\/\+Tidy before submitting. Supported tags are\+: a, b, blockquote, br, dd, del, div, dl, dt, em, font, h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6, hr, i, img, li, ol, p, pre, small, span, strong, sub, sup, table, tcpdf, td, th, thead, tr, tt, u, ul NOTE\+: all the HTML attributes must be enclosed in double-\/quote. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
string & {\em \$html} & text to display \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$ln} & if true add a new line after text (default = true) \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$fill} & Indicates if the background must be painted (true) or transparent (false). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$reseth} & if true reset the last cell height (default false). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$cell} & if true add the current left (or right for RTL) padding to each Write (default false). \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Allows to center or align the text. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L \+: left align
\item C \+: center
\item R \+: right align
\item \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} \+: empty string \+: left for LTR or right for RTL
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{figure}
\Hypertarget{class_t_c_p_d_f_aa5f289d5c4341e38727e9c8ab625fb10}\label{class_t_c_p_d_f_aa5f289d5c4341e38727e9c8ab625fb10} 
\index{TCPDF@{TCPDF}!writeHTMLCell@{writeHTMLCell}}
\index{writeHTMLCell@{writeHTMLCell}!TCPDF@{TCPDF}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{writeHTMLCell()}{writeHTMLCell()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily write\+HTMLCell (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{\$w,  }\item[{}]{\$h,  }\item[{}]{\$x,  }\item[{}]{\$y,  }\item[{}]{\$html = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$border = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$ln = {\ttfamily 0},  }\item[{}]{\$fill = {\ttfamily false},  }\item[{}]{\$reseth = {\ttfamily true},  }\item[{}]{\$align = {\ttfamily \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{}},  }\item[{}]{\$autopadding = {\ttfamily true} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyVerb}   Prints a cell (rectangular area) with optional borders, background color and html text string.
   The upper-left corner of the cell corresponds to the current position. After the call, the current position moves to the right or to the next line.<br />
   If automatic page breaking is enabled and the cell goes beyond the limit, a page break is done before outputting.
   IMPORTANT: The HTML must be well formatted - try to clean-up it using an application like HTML-Tidy before submitting.
   Supported tags are: a, b, blockquote, br, dd, del, div, dl, dt, em, font, h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6, hr, i, img, li, ol, p, pre, small, span, strong, sub, sup, table, tcpdf, td, th, thead, tr, tt, u, ul
   NOTE: all the HTML attributes must be enclosed in double-quote.
   @param float $w Cell width. If 0, the cell extends up to the right margin.
   @param float $h Cell minimum height. The cell extends automatically if needed.
   @param float|null $x upper-left corner X coordinate
   @param float|null $y upper-left corner Y coordinate
   @param string $html html text to print. Default value: empty string.
   @param mixed $border Indicates if borders must be drawn around the cell. The value can be a number:<ul><li>0: no border (default)</li><li>1: frame</li></ul> or a string containing some or all of the following characters (in any order):<ul><li>L: left</li><li>T: top</li><li>R: right</li><li>B: bottom</li></ul> or an array of line styles for each border group - for example: array('LTRB' => array('width' => 2, 'cap' => 'butt', 'join' => 'miter', 'dash' => 0, 'color' => array(0, 0, 0)))
   @param int $ln Indicates where the current position should go after the call. Possible values are:<ul><li>0: to the right (or left for RTL language)</li><li>1: to the beginning of the next line</li><li>2: below</li></ul>
\end{DoxyVerb}
 Putting 1 is equivalent to putting 0 and calling \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a61ced26209917509b2315cd23d650b55}{Ln()} just after. Default value\+: 0. 
\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Paramètres}
boolean & {\em \$fill} & Indicates if the cell background must be painted (true) or transparent (false). \\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$reseth} & if true reset the last cell height (default true). \\
\hline
string & {\em \$align} & Allows to center or align the text. Possible values are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L \+: left align
\item C \+: center
\item R \+: right align
\item \textquotesingle{}\textquotesingle{} \+: empty string \+: left for LTR or right for RTL
\end{DoxyItemize}\\
\hline
boolean & {\em \$autopadding} & if true, uses internal padding and automatically adjust it to account for line width. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{Voir également}
\doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a77b973d137fb33212e018b042df6e3e7}{Multicell()}, \doxylink{class_t_c_p_d_f_a59fedc90bb3a10d07cd476e7d282b2db}{write\+HTML()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
